The enqueue's broad `except Exception` backstop (§14) guarantees a teacher upload is never broken; a genuine enqueue regression is logged (`provisioning_enqueue_skipped`) — a candidate for a production alert. `promote`/`PromoteResult`/`run_provisioning`/`ProvisioningOutcome`/`enqueue_provisioning_job` are RE-EXPORTED from `apollo/provisioning/__init__.py`. The three mutation proofs (content-hash short-circuit, lease-reaper/terminal-status, intra-job no-op) + the flag-OFF byte-identical upload non-regression + the full-promote-spine re-home/gate-8 end-to-end (`test_full_promote_spine_rehomes_and_dedups_real_pg` — REAL `tag_and_mint`+`promote` through the positional-string adapter, project_canon mocked) are pinned in `tests/database/test_apollo_provisioning_orchestration.py` (real-PG, GREEN-not-skipped). **WU-3B2h — the §8B.3 per-problem anomaly-quarantine backstop (the spec-CLOSING unit).** Two new files: `quarantine_constants.py` pins the three hand-set v1 thresholds `N_MIN=8` / `THETA_MISS=0.80` / `CONCENTRATION_MARGIN=0.40` (all env-overridable `APOLLO_QUARANTINE_*` for calibration, committed defaults pinned by tests); `quarantine.py` ships `quarantine_decision(coverage_matrix, *, n_min, theta_miss, margin) -> QuarantineVerdict` (a PURE, DB/IO/LLM-free, immutable miss-concentration statistic over a hand-buildable `{node_key -> per-attempt missing? flags}` matrix — fires iff ALL THREE clauses hold: `N >= n_min`, `m(top) >= theta_miss`, and `m(top) - mean_m >= margin`; each clause independently mutation-proven; stdlib `statistics` ONLY, NO numpy/scipy) PLUS the async real-PG `sweep_quarantine(db, *, search_space_id=None) -> SweepReport`. The sweep runs the **§9 OPS-3 aggregation join** — `apollo_graph_comparison_findings` (WHERE `finding_kind='missing_node'`, LOAD-BEARING/mutation-proven) → `apollo_graph_comparison_runs` → `apollo_problem_attempts`, where `attempts.problem_id` is **TEXT == `problem_code`** (NOT the BIGINT id); the **per-node key is `findings.reference_node_ids`** (a JSONB list), NOT `entity_id`: the PRODUCTION grading core (`apollo/grading/persistence.py` `finding_to_row_spec`) hardcodes `entity_id=NULL` in v1 and carries the missing reference node's identity in `reference_node_ids` (== the canonical reference node's source step ids; `apollo/graph_compare/findings.py` `missing_finding`), so keying on the always-NULL `entity_id` would make quarantine **INERT against real data** (this was a review blocker — the sweep keys on `reference_node_ids` precisely so it consumes what the grader emits). The sweep derives a stable per-node key via `_node_key` (a JSON-canonical sorted string over `reference_node_ids`); a finding with an EMPTY `reference_node_ids` carries no resolvable node identity and is EXCLUDED (`_node_key` → `None`) so it never becomes a phantom node (mutation-proven by `test_sweep_ignores_empty_reference_node_ids_findings`). N (the denominator) = `COUNT(DISTINCT runs.attempt_id)` per `(problem_code, search_space_id)`, and per-node `miss_count` is CLAMPED to N (`min`) so >1 missing_node finding for the SAME node in one attempt cannot produce a ragged matrix / dict-order-dependent N (mutation-proven by `test_sweep_clamps_multiple_findings_per_attempt_for_same_node`); the TEXT problem_code resolves to the **BIGINT** `apollo_concept_problems` row via `cp.search_space_id = runs.search_space_id AND cp.problem_code = attempts.problem_id` (course-scoped by `runs.search_space_id`, no cross-course leak), and the sweep stamps/clears `cp.quarantined_at` REVERSIBLY (re-cleared as N grows and the concentration no longer fires), commits once, and emits one structured audit row per fire (`event=quarantine_fire` with `problem_code`/`search_space_id`/`node_key`/`n_attempts`/`top_miss_rate`/`concentration`) or clear (`event=quarantine_clear`). It is best-effort observability infra: an orphan finding (no matching concept_problems row) is logged `event=quarantine_resolution_miss` at WARNING and skipped, never raised. **§9 OPS-4 KNOWN LIMIT (documented honestly, NOT over-claimed):** the simple miss-concentration rule WILL false-quarantine a genuinely-hard prerequisite node legitimately missed by most students — it has the SAME signature as a mispaired reference solution and v1 does NOT distinguish them. The three v1 mitigations are (a) **reversibility** (the re-clear path), (b) the **per-fire audit log** so a human can review false positives, and (c) treating quarantine as **ADVISORY** until the ADJ #12 calibration step passes before any `APOLLO_AUTOPROVISION_ENABLED` flip; the point-biserial discrimination refinement (a hard node has POSITIVE point-biserial, a mispaired reference near-zero/negative) is **v1.1** (ADJ #1 / ADJ #8) — deliberately NOT built here. NO migration (`quarantined_at` shipped in migration 030/WU-3B2a), NO new package. Tests: `apollo/provisioning/tests/test_quarantine.py` + `test_quarantine_constants.py` (pure, fixture-only) and `tests/database/test_apollo_quarantine_shadow.py` (real-PG, GREEN-not-skipped — the sweep aggregation/resolution/reversibility/idempotence/audit-log/`missing_node`-filter-mutation/empty-`reference_node_ids`-guard/`miss_count`-clamp tests + the selector-exclusion test + the §9 SPEC-4 shadow invariant + the `test_shadow_findings_feed_sweep_end_to_end` BRIDGE that runs the real shadow `handle_done` and proves its `entity_id=NULL`/`reference_node_ids`-keyed findings actually feed the sweep end-to-end). **G4.3 (lane B2.3) — mint-time content dedup + equation payloads:** BEFORE the ladder runs, `_collapse_equivalent_candidates` folds reference candidates minted from ONE authored set that share a deterministic `_equivalence_signature(spec) = (kind, tier, content)` onto ONE representative (`content` = the sign-canonical `_normalize_equation` for equations, else the RAW `payload['symbol']`, else a whitespace-collapsed `display_name`). Folded keys are surfaced on `MintPlan.collapsed_entity_keys`, do NOT mint a row, and each aliases to its representative's entity id in `key_to_id` so a prereq/opposes edge naming a duplicate still resolves. So BEFORE the per-candidate ladder, `tag_and_mint` loads this concept's already-persisted rows (`tag_mint_persist.load_concept_entities`, `concept_id`-scoped, ascending-id) and resolves any candidate whose `_equivalence_signature` EXACTLY matches a prior-upload row straight onto that row's id (first-writer-wins), recording it on `MintPlan.merged_entity_keys` and SKIPPING `resolve_candidate`. BACK-COMPAT: a concept minted BEFORE this rework may already hold cross-upload duplicates — they are NOT retroactively merged; new candidates dedup against the FIRST (lowest-id) surviving row. |
| `apollo/graph_compare/` | `validator.py`, `canonical.py`, `problem_inputs.py`, `coverage.py`, `soundness.py`, `scores.py`, `bisimilarity.py`, `findings.py`, `core.py`, `__init__.py` | The **§6 grading core** (WU-4A1 BUILD half + WU-4A2 COMPARE half) — the pure, DB-free, LLM-free, frozen-dataclass package that mirrors `apollo/resolution/` and consumes it. **BUILD half (WU-4A1):** `validator.py`/`canonical.py`/`problem_inputs.py`. It (1) **validates the raw graphs**: `validate_student_graph` is the §6.4 step-4 gate — re-derives each edge's endpoint node types from the graph's `node_index()` (parser edges may carry `None` type fields, so the optional `from_node_type`/`to_node_type` are NOT trusted), then checks `EDGE_ALLOWED_PAIRS`, endpoint existence, `attempt_id` scoping uniformity (all nodes + edges one id), and no PRECEDES cycle (via `KGGraph.topological_order`); `validate_reference` is the §6.6 gate and DELEGATES to `learner_model_seed.validate_reference_graph` (REUSE — never reimplements §6.1). (2) builds **`S_norm`** (`build_student_canonical(student_graph, resolution)`): MERGES student nodes by `resolved_key` (two nodes resolving to the same target collapse into ONE `CanonicalNode` carrying both raw node-ids (sorted) + evidence spans, deterministic method/confidence via highest-cap tie-break), normalizes edges to canonical endpoints, **DROPS** an edge with an unresolved endpoint (counting it in `dropped_edge_count`, never silently), and **RETAINS** unresolved student nodes as `unresolved_nodes` findings-input (§6.3). (3) builds **`R_norm`** (`build_reference_canonical(problem)`): one node per `reference_solution` step (keyed on `entity_key`), the dependency DAG from each step's `depends_on`, and one `ReferencePathView` per `declared_paths` entry — **from the problem's OWN reference_solution ONLY**, NEVER the deduped `apollo_kg_entities` payload (Decision 3 regression guard). (4) assembles resolver inputs (`build_problem_candidates`) — the closed candidate set (REUSING the WU-3C2 builders) + the per-problem `symbolic_mappings` table. **COMPARE half (WU-4A2):** `coverage.py`/`soundness.py`/`scores.py`/`bisimilarity.py`/`findings.py`/`core.py`. The single public callable `grade_attempt(student_canonical, reference_graph) -> GradeResult` (§6.4 steps 10/11/13) consumes the two WU-4A1 canonical graphs and produces a frozen `GradeResult` (3 top-line + 7 sub-scores) + in-memory `Finding`s. Binding rules: **coverage = MAX over declared paths** (`R ⊑ S` per path — a student on a valid alternative path is graded against the path they took, never punished against the authored one; missing findings emitted ONLY against the WINNING path); **soundness = contradictions-only** (`S ⊑ R` — a contradiction is an S_norm node whose key starts with `misc.`, `1 - 0.5·k` capped at 0; **unsupported extras + unresolved nodes carry ZERO soundness penalty**); the **7 sub-scores** (procedure_order penalizes only true PRECEDES inversions read off the winning path SEQUENCE, never a missing stated order; dependency is the lowest-weight direction-loose DEPENDS_ON; **edges are diagnostic-only and explicit outweighs inferred** (`INFERRED_EDGE_WEIGHT=0.5`)); **bisimilarity = harmonic_mean(soundness, coverage)** with `a+b==0 → 0`, NEVER NaN. **Edges NEVER produce events and never move the three top-line scores.** It computes scores but **persists nothing, runs NO Neo4j/Postgres/LLM, and emits NO events** — finding→event conversion (§6.5), abstention gates, transcript audit, and the runs/findings persistence are WU-4B (which also supplies the persisted `normalization_confidence`); the live `resolve_attempt` call + Done-route wiring are WU-4C. Named errors `StudentGraphInvalidError`/`ReferenceGraphInvalidError` (carry a `reasons` tuple; deliberately NOT HTTP-registered here — the Done route is WU-4C). |
| `apollo/grading/` | `transcript_audit.py`, `abstention.py`, `audited_grade.py`, `event_model.py`, `opposes.py`, `events.py`, `normalization_confidence.py`, `reference_hash.py`, `persistence.py`, `rubric_mapping.py`, `calibration.py`, `diagnostic.py`, `fixtures/corpus.py`, `__init__.py` | The §6 grading **downstream layer** (WU-4B) — the LLM/IO-coupled orchestration that CONSUMES the pure `graph_compare` score core (it IMPORTS `graph_compare`, never extends it; mirrors `resolution/`(pure) vs `resolution_store.py`(IO)). **WU-4B1 ships §6.4 step 12 (transcript audit) + step 14 (§6.6 abstention).** `transcript_audit.py`: `audit_missing()` runs ONE batched `main_chat` call (never per-node; chunked to a char budget) over the simulator-flagged `missing_node` entities + the raw transcript, upgrading a `missing` finding to a covered-grade finding ONLY when the audit quotes a supporting span — at a NAMED `TRANSCRIPT_AUDIT_CONFIDENCE_CAP = 0.75` (equals the `llm` method cap; a grading-package constant, NEVER a key added to the frozen resolution `METHOD_CONFIDENCE_CAP` — anti-laundering: the learned alias resolves at 0.75, NOT the 0.92 alias tier, until a teacher approves it). Any audit-infra failure (timeout / JSON-parse / empty payload) raises the named `TranscriptAuditUnavailableError` (in `errors.py`, mirrors `ResolutionUnavailableError`, NO FALLBACK) — NEVER "skip audit and emit the missing finding". `main_chat_auditor` is the live default `audit_fn`; tests inject a deterministic stub so no live LLM fires. `abstention.py`: `apply_abstention()` applies the §6.6 gates — `unresolved_rate > 0.35` → `abstained` (the no-Layer-3-update run); **Phase 1c quality brake: `normalization_confidence < ABSTENTION_THRESHOLDS["min_normalization_confidence"] = 0.85` → `abstained` (the SECOND trigger besides `unresolved_rate` that sets the flag) + `REASON_LOW_NORMALIZATION_CONFIDENCE`** — keyed on resolution *quality* (the weakest-link nc), NOT *success*, so an attempt resolving only via weak tiers (`fuzzy@0.80`/`llm@0.75`) still abstains even after Phase 1a/1b lower `unresolved_rate`; the floor sits ABOVE `derived@0.95`/`alias@0.92` (only the weak tiers trip it) and is calibration-owned (spec §10 — NOT raised to "catch derived"); the gate takes a keyword-only `normalization_confidence: float = 1.0` whose default never trips (backward-compatible at all call sites); **MIN parser_confidence (NEVER mean) `< 0.6` → suppress `missing`**; transcript-audit failure → suppress ALL `missing`; any misconception resolution confidence `< 0.8` → withhold `misconception` (the finding still persists for review); reference-invalid → recorded (grading already blocked upstream) — returning the `abstention_reasons` tuple (deterministic gate-declaration order: unresolved → normalization → parser → audit → misconception → ref) + `abstained` flag + the per-event-kind suppression set (the kinds WU-4B2 must withhold). `audited_grade.py`: `build_audited_grade()` orchestrates step 12+14 into the frozen `AuditedGrade` handoff (the `GradeResult` carried UNCHANGED + audit-upgraded findings as a NEW immutable tuple + `abstention_reasons` + `abstained` + emitted `AliasCandidate` value objects); it CATCHES `TranscriptAuditUnavailableError` at the audit boundary and routes it to suppress-all-`missing` (proof it was handled, not silently swallowed). **Phase 1c D1 reorder:** the orchestration tail now `_rewrite_findings` FIRST → computes `normalization_confidence = _normalization_confidence_over(new_findings, resolution)` over the POST-rewrite findings → passes it into `apply_abstention(..., normalization_confidence=...)` → constructs `AuditedGrade`. nc is computed over POST-rewrite findings because an audit upgrade turns a `missing_node` into a SCORED `covered_node`, so the gate must see the same finding set the persisted value does — `done_grading.py` calls `compute_normalization_confidence(audited, resolution)` over `audited.findings` (already rewritten here), so the internal gate nc is **byte-identical** to the persisted `apollo_graph_comparison_runs.normalization_confidence` (Phase 1c only GATES on nc, never changes it). `_misconception_confidences` stays over `grade.findings` (PRE-rewrite) — `_rewrite_findings` only touches `missing_node`→`covered_node`, so the `contradiction` findings the misconception gate keys on are identical pre/post. `build_audited_grade`'s SIGNATURE is unchanged (the nc is an internal local, not a new kwarg). Produces NO events (finding→event §6.5 is **WU-4B2**), persists NOTHING (runs/findings + `abstention_reasons`/`abstained` writes are **WU-4B3**), and emits `AliasCandidate` value objects only (the §8 teacher-approval queue is **WU-3B2**). The error is named-but-not-HTTP-registered (WU-4C registers the Done-route handler). **WU-4B2 ships §6.4 step 16 (finding→event, §6.5 decision table).** `event_model.py`: the frozen `LearnerEvent` (maps onto `apollo_mastery_events` columns — `canonical_key`/`event_kind`/`score`/`confidence`/`misconception_code`/`evidence_node_ids`/`reference_step_id`; the parser/grader/belief columns are WU-5A's at the belief update, NOT here) + `LearnerEventKind` StrEnum (value-set == `models.MASTERY_EVENT_KINDS`, asserted) + `EVENT_CONVERSION_VERSION` (`"finding-to-event-v1"`). `opposes.py`: `build_opposes_map(candidates) -> {misc_key: opposed_key}` from each misconception `Candidate.opposes_key` (§6.5: opposes-links make the conflict rows detectable). `events.py`: `convert_findings_to_events(audited_grade, *, opposes_map, turn_order) -> tuple[LearnerEvent, ...]` applies the BINDING §6.5 table — covered(+edges)→`covered` scaled by resolution confidence; covered+edge-missing STAYS `covered` (the `partial` variant is calibration-gated OFF behind `PARTIAL_EDGE_GAP_ENABLED=False` — an edge gap must never halve a score, §6.2; `edge-gap` is a declared-but-dormant flag); missing_node+audit-negative→`missing` s=0.0; the audit-upgrade row keys on the `AUDIT_UPGRADE_MESSAGE` MARKER (NOT kind/confidence — a genuine llm-tier covered also sits at 0.75)→`covered` ≤0.75; contradiction→`misconception` s=0.0; CONFLICT rows use `opposes_map` + the INJECTED `turn_order` (node_id→turn position; supplied by WU-4C from `apollo_messages.turn_index`/Neo4j `created_at`, by fixtures in tests — 4B2 stays PURE over it, never queries Postgres/Neo4j; per-finding turn = `min` over its `student_node_ids`, absent id → `+inf` sentinel): contradiction-earlier+covered-later→`corrected` on the opposed entity; covered-earlier+contradiction-later→`misconception` (last position wins); ambiguous/equal order→`partial` + `mixed-understanding` flag. **Multi-opposer** (two misconceptions opposing the SAME covered entity — a spec gap) is generalized to last-position-wins against the LATEST opposer, emitting EXACTLY ONE event per covered entity (consuming the covered key + all its opposers) so the WU-5A `UNIQUE (attempt_id, entity_id, event_kind)` can never collide. `unsupported_extra`/`unresolved`/matched_edge/missing_edge/alternative_path→NO event. Honors WU-4B1's abstention: `abstained` →`()` (no learner update at all); else DROPS events whose kind ∈ `suppressed_event_kinds` (`corrected` survives a `misconception` suppression — distinct kind), applied LAST after conflict resolution. Output sorted by `(canonical_key, event_kind.value)` (deterministic). Produces in-memory events ONLY — event PERSISTENCE (atomic write with the 3-state Bayesian belief update + parser/grader/belief columns) is **WU-5A**; the `turn_order` SOURCE query + Done wiring + §6.7 shadow/§6.8 diagnostics are **WU-4C**; runs/findings persistence is **WU-4B3**. **WU-4B3 ships §6.4 step 15 (runs+findings persistence, supersede) + the §3 damper input + the reference-graph fingerprint + the §6.11 executable corpus** — mirroring `resolution/`(pure) vs `resolution_store.py`(IO): pure `*_to_row` spec dataclasses (DB-free, 1:1 column mapping, testable without a container) + a thin async write seam. `persistence.py`: the frozen `RunRowSpec`/`FindingRowSpec` value objects (1:1 `apollo_graph_comparison_runs`/`_findings` columns, NO id/created_at) + `grade_to_run_spec`/`finding_to_row_spec`/`findings_to_row_specs` (the 10 `*_score` fields copy 1:1 from `GradeResult`; `abstained`/`abstention_reasons` come from `AuditedGrade`, NOT recomputed; tuples→JSONB lists; `student_edge_ids`/`reference_edge_ids` always `[]` — edges are message-only; `entity_id` is NULL in v1 — the canonical_key→`apollo_kg_entities.id` join is not a WU-4B3 concern, `ON DELETE SET NULL` tolerates NULL). `persist_comparison_run(db, *, attempt_id, user_id, search_space_id, grade, audited, normalization_confidence, reference_graph_hash) -> run_id` persists the run + one findings row per **`audited.findings`** (the audit-REWRITTEN set — an audit-upgraded missing→covered persists as the COVERED it became, carrying the span + capped 0.75 + `AUDIT_UPGRADE_MESSAGE`; persisting `grade.findings` would lose the upgrade) with **SUPERSEDE** in ONE transaction (DELETE the prior run at `(attempt_id, comparison_version)` → its findings CASCADE → reinsert; a legit retry NEVER crashes on the `UNIQUE(attempt_id, comparison_version)`; DELETE+INSERT share one txn so the supersede is atomic), persists **ALWAYS** including abstained runs (`abstained=true`, findings still written — §6.4 step 15 persist-always), and does **NOT** `commit()` — the caller (WU-4C `done.py`) owns the txn boundary (it `flush()`es so the `run_id` is real + FK-valid within the open transaction). `normalization_confidence.py`: `compute_normalization_confidence(audited_grade, resolution) -> float` is the §3 damper input — the conservative **MIN (weakest-link)** over the per-node method-cap `ResolvedNode.confidence` of the resolved nodes backing a SCORED finding (`_SCORED_FINDING_KINDS = {covered_node, contradiction}`; `unsupported_extra`/`unresolved`/edges are diagnostic-only ⇒ excluded), returning the named knob `NORMALIZATION_CONFIDENCE_FLOOR_WHEN_NO_SCORED_NODES = 1.0` when no scored finding has a resolved backer (no scored evidence ⇒ nothing to damp ⇒ neutral, NOT 0.0). It feeds `grader_confidence = normalization_confidence × comparison_confidence` (§3 line 431); exported for WU-4C to call at the `done.py` call site (NOT called inside `persist_comparison_run`, which takes the scalar so it stays pure-mappable). **Phase 1c** extracted the MIN-over-scored-backers body into a pure helper `_normalization_confidence_over(findings, resolution) -> float` (takes the findings tuple DIRECTLY, so `build_audited_grade` can compute nc over POST-rewrite findings before the frozen `AuditedGrade` exists); `compute_normalization_confidence` is now a thin delegator over `audited_grade.findings` (signature/name/value preserved). To avoid the runtime import cycle this creates (`audited_grade` now imports the helper at runtime), the `AuditedGrade` import in `normalization_confidence.py` moved under `if TYPE_CHECKING:` (safe — `from __future__ import annotations` makes the public function's parameter annotation a string at runtime). `reference_hash.py`: `reference_graph_hash(reference_graph) -> str` is a deterministic **STABLE** sorted-canonical sha256 over the `ReferenceGraph` AS GRADED — nodes `(canonical_key, node_type, symbolic)` (step ids/evidence_spans excluded so a step-id rename keeps the hash stable) + edges `(edge_type, from_key, to_key)` + path key-tuples, order-independent via `json.dumps(sort_keys=True)` (NEVER builtin `hash()`/`repr`), version-prefixed `REFERENCE_HASH_VERSION = "refhash-v1"`; STABLE across replays (old runs stay explainable) + SENSITIVE to any node/edge/path change (a teacher edit changes the hash, §2). `fixtures/corpus.py`: the **§6.11 executable corpus** — 12 adversarial `CorpusFixture` rows + the §6.9 Bernoulli capstone, each shipping expected audited findings AND expected events, driving `build_audited_grade → convert_findings_to_events` (deterministic resolution + injected `audit_fn`, no live LLM) by COMPOSING the upstream `_builders.py` helpers; the persistence-touching rows (parser-miss, high-unresolved abstention, Bernoulli) are exercised on REAL PG (`tests/database/test_apollo_comparison_run_persistence.py` + `..._corpus_persistence.py`: round-trip all columns + abstention_reasons JSONB + nullable sub-scores + supersede CASCADE + abstained-persist + FK integrity). The runs/findings tables (migration-026 ORM) are now **WRITTEN** by WU-4B3 (no longer "schema only, nothing reads/writes them"). **WU-4C2 adds the graph-sim candidate-grade harness — `rubric_mapping.py`, `calibration.py`, `diagnostic.py` (PURE + LLM-MOCK, NO DB/Neo4j/migration).** `rubric_mapping.py`: `findings_to_rubric_input(*, audited, reference_graph, opposes_map, turn_order) -> RubricMappingInput` + `build_graph_sim_rubric(*, ...) -> dict` map `AuditedGrade.findings` + the graph-sim `ReferenceGraph` onto the FROZEN `compute_rubric` input bag (keyed on `canonical_key`, bridged via the duck-typed `RubricRefNode{node_id, node_type}` so no heavy `ontology.Node` import) and CALL `compute_rubric` (no reimplementation — mirrors the OLD path's call shape); `misconception_scores` derive 0.5 (detected-unresolved) / 1.0 (a CONTRADICTION whose `opposes_map` target has a COVERED finding asserted LATER by `turn_order`) — RECON #7: `opposes_map` is structurally EMPTY today so real data lands at 0.5, the 1.0 branch is exercised with a SYNTHETIC opposes fixture; a private `_turn_position` COPIES the events.py min-over-`student_node_ids` SHAPE (not imported — the rubric axis stays decoupled from the §6.5 event table). `calibration.py`: `compute_calibration_metrics(*, old_rubric, shadow_rubric) -> CalibrationMetrics` (§6.7) — letter agreement (reads `["overall"]["letter"]` directly, NEVER recomputes), `overall_score_delta = shadow - old`, per-axis `AxisDelta` over `overall` + `rubric.AXIS_WEIGHTS` keys (an axis `present=False` on a side ⇒ `None` score/delta, no spurious 0-agreement), and `divergent` (the human-review trip wire: letters disagree OR `|overall_score_delta| > DIVERGENCE_SCORE_THRESHOLD = 10`); `CALIBRATION_VERSION = "calibration-v1"`. NO new column / NO persistence — the metrics are LOGGED + carried in-memory on `ShadowGradeResult` (WU-4C key_decision #6 reuses JSONB; a calibration table is a later concern). `diagnostic.py`: the §6.8 CONSTRAINED, findings-only diagnostic — `generate_constrained_diagnostic(audited, *, llm=None) -> ConstrainedDiagnostic` builds a `DiagnosticRequest` from FINDINGS ONLY (covered/missing/misconception keys + quoted `evidence_spans`, NEVER the raw transcript — there is intentionally NO `transcript` field, the §6.8 "structurally unable to re-grade" guarantee), runs an INJECTED `llm` callable (default `main_chat_diagnostic_llm`, which lazily imports `OpenAI` inside its body — NO top-level OpenAI import, CI-safe), and applies a deterministic PURE POST-CHECK (no covered-verb governing a missing key; no `misc.*` token absent from `misconception_keys`; evidence-span reference is SOFT, never a hard fail) with regenerate-once-then-deterministic-template fallback (`used_fallback=True`, logged at WARNING — NO-FALLBACK-but-degrade; an llm that raises both times also falls back, never bubbling into the Done route). DISTINCT from the FROZEN `overseer/diagnostic.py` (which stays on the OLD student-facing path with its direct `OpenAI()` call — UNTOUCHED). `__init__.py` re-exports the new names ADDITIVELY (the WU-4B1/4B2/4B3 names stay). **Campaign-plan Task A2 adds `composite.py` + `artifact_build.py`** (PURE — no DB/Neo4j/LLM imports), the canonical-grading-artifact builders that feed migration 034's `GradingArtifact` (Task A1). `composite.py`: the frozen `CompositeWeights(w_n, w_e, p)` + `load_weights()` (env `APOLLO_COMPOSITE_W_NODE`/`_W_EDGE`/`_P_MISC`, defaults `0.6`/`0.25`/`0.15`, read fresh per call — no process caching, so campaign tuning runs can flip env between attempts) + `composite_score(node_coverage, edge_coverage, misconception_penalty, weights) -> float` implementing the spec §1/Q5 formula `w_n*node_coverage + w_e*edge_coverage - p*misconception_penalty`, clamped to `[0,1]` and rounded to 6dp; `MISC_CONFIDENCE_FLOOR = 0.5` is the named misconception-assertion confidence floor. `artifact_build.py`: `build_graph_artifact(*, shadow: ShadowGradeResult, weights, clarification_trace, latency_ms) -> dict` and `build_llm_artifact(*, coverage, rubric, weights, graph_failure, latency_ms, clarification_trace, misconceptions_bank_empty=False) -> dict` — both return the ARTIFACT PAYLOAD dict (node/edge ledgers, misconceptions, scores, versions, abstention block) that Task A3's Done-click writer merges with the identity columns (`attempt_id`/`user_id`/`search_space_id`/`concept_id`/`problem_id`/`role`) it alone knows. The graph node ledger is built from `shadow.audited.findings` (the post-audit-rewrite set, same as `persist_comparison_run` writes): `COVERED_NODE`→`credited`, `CONTRADICTION`→`misconception`, `UNRESOLVED`→`unresolved`; `MISSING_NODE` → `unresolved` too (scorecard fix below). Resolution METHOD (a `Finding` has none) is looked up from the WIDENED `ShadowGradeResult.resolution` field (below) by matching `ResolvedNode.resolved_key == finding.canonical_key`; `CREDITED_METHODS` excludes `llm` (the transcript-audit upgrade tier, tracked via `AUDIT_UPGRADE_MESSAGE`, not the resolver) and `unresolved`. The edge ledger parses `MATCHED_EDGE`/`MISSING_EDGE` finding messages (`"<from> -<TYPE>-> <to> (<provenance>)"`) into `{from_key, edge_type, to_key, provenance, status}`, degrading to all-`None` on a malformed/missing message rather than raising (edges are diagnostic-only). `misconception_penalty = compute_misconception_penalty(...)` = (count of `CONTRADICTION` findings with confidence >= `MISC_CONFIDENCE_FLOOR`) / `max(1, reference_node_count)`, where `reference_node_count` is derived from the findings themselves (every real reference node is exactly one of `COVERED_NODE`/`MISSING_NODE` on the winning path, §6.4 step 8 — no separate count needed). `build_llm_artifact` is coarser by design (spec §3): nodes come straight off `coverage["per_step"]` (the REAL `compute_coverage` return shape — a `{node_id: "covered"|"missing"}` map; an EARLIER build wrongly read a fictional `coverage["covered"]`/`["missing"]` list pair that never exists, silently zeroing `node_coverage`/`composite`/`node_ledger` on every LLM-fallback attempt — fixed campaign-plan Task T1), no method per node and `evidence_span=None` per node (Q2/lane B4 fix, 2026-07-02 campaign: the LLM grader produces per-node coverage but NO per-node student utterance — `per_step` carries no surface text and there is no deterministic node→step→utterance mapping to recover one without an extra LLM call, so `None` is the honest "no span available" value, matching the `_missing_ledger_entry` convention; PREVIOUSLY `""`, which rendered as a fake empty quote in every scorecard and, being non-null, was wrongly excluded from `struggle_signals`' reference-key coverage; the `evidence_span` KEY stays present with value `null` so the S3 fidelity judge's `.get('evidence_span')` input shape is unchanged), edge ledger is always `[]`, `misconception_penalty` is always `0.0`, `grader_used="llm_fallback"`, and the abstention block carries `graph_failure` (the any-exception-caught reason, Task A4). **A2/G2 fix (2026-07-03 campaign): `clarification_trace` is threaded through exactly like `build_graph_artifact` — clarifications are SESSION-level evidence (the student's live answer-blind follow-up dialog), not grader-specific. PREVIOUSLY `build_llm_artifact` hardcoded `clarification_trace=[]` unconditionally; since `served` is `llm_fallback` on every attempt today (the graph grader is still shadow), the SERVED canonical artifact and the student/teacher scorecard (`render_scorecard(canonical_payload)`, `done.py:664`) NEVER showed clarifications even when the live loop ran and produced real exchanges (F1c DB evidence: 34/36 `pair` rows carried a nonempty trace, 0/36 `canonical` rows did). `write_artifacts` now passes the SAME `_load_clarification_trace` result into both builders — real trace when rows exist, `[]` (never `None`) otherwise, matching the graph path's convention.** Because the LLM path has no edge/misconception decomposition, `scores.composite` for this grader does NOT run through the graph path's weighted `composite_score` formula (which tops out at `w_n` when edge/misconception are both 0, silently capping every LLM-graded attempt below "Strong") — it is instead the ALREADY-COMPUTED rubric's `overall.score` (0-100) renormalized to the artifact's `[0,1]` scale (spec §3: "Same scorecard shape either way — LLM grade rendered into the same band"), so the canonical artifact's band always matches the grade actually served to the student. `node_coverage` is still reported (informational parity with the graph artifact's shape) but does not feed `composite` on this path. **`ShadowGradeResult` (in `apollo/handlers/done_grading.py`) is WIDENED (Task A2 Step 3) with a REQUIRED `resolution: ResolutionResult` field** (no default, same WU-4C2 rationale — a half-populated ledger basis is a silent bug), populated in `run_graph_simulation` from the SAME `resolve_attempt(...)` call already made (no new computation) — every existing construction site (`test_subject_fluid_teachback.py`, `tests/database/test_done_layer3_route_postgres.py`) updated additively. **Scorecard fix (code-review medium finding)** — `build_node_ledger` originally EXCLUDED `MISSING_NODE` findings entirely (a reference node with ZERO student evidence — nothing was said), reasoning that `node_coverage` already reflected it; in practice this meant the student/teacher scorecard's "missing or unclear" rubric block (`apollo.projections.scorecard._missing_or_unclear`, which reads straight off `node_ledger`) had NOTHING to show for a concept the student never touched at all — "nothing computed fresh" (spec §2) means the ledger has to carry it. Chosen fix (Option A over a separate `missing_reference_nodes` block — less invasive: no new artifact-schema key, no new consumer to wire, the existing `unresolved`-status renderer already generalizes): `_missing_ledger_entry(finding)` now emits one `unresolved` node-ledger row per `MISSING_NODE` finding, keyed by the REFERENCE node's own display-safe `canonical_key` (`missing_finding` already sets this from `ref_node.canonical_key` — never an internal student-side id, unlike the pre-existing `UNRESOLVED`-utterance `unresolved` row, which is keyed by a student node id since there IS no reference key for an utterance that matched nothing) with `evidence_span`/`confidence` explicitly `None` (not `""`/`0.0`) so a row backed by a REAL failed resolution attempt stays distinguishable from one backed by NO attempt at all. `apollo.projections.mastery._ledger_entity_keys` filters to `status IN ('credited','misconception')`, so it is unaffected by (correctly excludes) the new `unresolved` rows — no ripple into Task B2. `apollo.projections.classroom.struggle_signals`' `lowest_coverage_nodes` aggregate (review fix, Task B3) ALSO now includes an `unresolved` row when `evidence_span IS NULL` — that null is exactly the `_missing_ledger_entry` signature (a REAL failed resolution attempt always carries a span string, even empty; only "never attempted" is `None`), so a MISSING_NODE-keyed row contributes a 0.0-coverage data point per reference `canonical_key` while a student-node-id-keyed `UNRESOLVED`-utterance row (which always carries a non-null `evidence_span`) stays excluded. |
| `apollo/learner_model/` | `belief.py`, `state_model.py`, `update.py`, `persistence.py`, `decay.py`, `negotiation.py`, `personalization_read.py`, `personalization_select.py`, `__init__.py` | **WU-5A1 — the PURE 3-state Bayesian filter core (§3 / §6.5 math), no IO** (NO DB/LLM/Neo4j/containers; consumes ONLY `apollo.grading.event_model` + `AMBIGUOUS_ORDER_SCORE`). The belief vector is `(p_misc, p_shaky, p_mastered)`. **`belief.py`**: cold-start prior `COLD_START_PRIOR=(0.20,0.60,0.20)`; the §6.5 likelihood table — covered at coverage `s` is `((1−s)^γ, 1−|2s−1|^γ, s^γ)` with the BKT boundary floor `LIKELIHOOD_FLOOR=0.02` clamped per-component (implements §3 line 427 "never 0" — kills the absorbing-zero on perfect-covered `s∈{0,1}`, where without it `L=(0,0,1)` would permanently annihilate `p_misc`), the fixed rows `MISSING=(0.7,1.0,0.4)`/`MISCONCEPTION=(3.0,1.0,0.2)`/`CORRECTED=(0.5,1.5,1.2)`, and `partial` maps to `covered@AMBIGUOUS_ORDER_SCORE` (=0.5, imported not re-literal'd); the §3.1 linear damper `damp(L,q)=q·L+(1−q)·(1,1,1)` (q=0→no-op, q=1→identity); `bayes_update` = normalize(prior⊙L) with a zero-sum guard (returns the prior); `mastery_of=0.5·p_shaky+p_mastered`; `confidence_of=1−entropy/log3` (the `if p>0` 0·log0 guard); and the TWO-STEP `misconception_code_of` (returns the code only once `p_misc` is the argmax AND `≥MISCONCEPTION_FLAG_THRESHOLD=0.5` AND the event carries a code — typically the 2nd misconception). γ=`GAMMA=1.5` (so `s=0.5`→argmax shaky, `s=0.25`→argmax misc). **`state_model.py`**: frozen `BeliefUpdate` (prior/posterior belief + mastery/confidence readouts + two-step misconception code + parser/grader confidences + recorded `dt_days_since_last`) / `MasteryEventRowSpec` (1:1 `apollo_mastery_events` non-id cols) / `LearnerStateRowSpec` (1:1 `apollo_learner_state` belief cols; `last_evidence_at` OMITTED — WU-5A2 sets it to `done_ts`). The identity columns (`user_id`/`search_space_id`/`entity_id`/`attempt_id`) default `None` — WU-5A1 does not resolve ids; WU-5A2 fills them (mirrors `FindingRowSpec.entity_id: int|None`). **`update.py`**: pure `apply_event(event, *, prior_belief, prior_last_evidence_at, parser_confidence, grader_confidence, done_ts) -> BeliefUpdate` — `q = parser_confidence·grader_confidence` ONLY (`event.confidence` is NOT re-multiplied: the COVERED `score` is already resolution-scaled by the §6.5 converter, so folding it in would double-count); cold-start when `prior_belief is None`; records `dt_days_since_last` (whole-day gap to `done_ts`, `None` when no anchor) but applies NO decay (decay is WU-5B) — plus `event_to_row_specs` (the WU-5A2 hand-off seam mapping `event`+`update` onto the two frozen row specs). **WU-5A2 adds `persistence.py` — the all-or-nothing Layer-3 write seam (REAL DB; mirrors `grading/persistence.py`'s flush-only supersede pattern).** `persist_learner_update(db, *, sess, attempt, shadow, done_ts, parser_confidence, canon_key_by_canonical_key) -> LearnerUpdateResult` is FLUSH-ONLY (the caller owns the txn boundary): it calls `convert_findings_to_events(shadow.audited, opposes_map=…, turn_order=…)` (§6.4 step 16 — the FIRST and ONLY caller; `done_grading.py`'s `test_no_mastery_events_written` tripwire stays green), resolves each event's `canonical_key -> entity_id` via the injected `{spec.canonical_key: spec.key}` map (an UNMAPPED key is SKIPPED into `LearnerUpdateResult.skipped_unmapped`, NEVER inserted with a NULL `entity_id`), attempt-wide SUPERSEDEs (`DELETE FROM apollo_mastery_events WHERE attempt_id = :id` — covers a misconception→corrected kind change across runs), `SELECT … FOR UPDATE`s the prior `apollo_learner_state` rows, recomputes the base from the EVENT LOG (the latest `posterior_belief` from a DIFFERENT attempt, `attempt_id IS DISTINCT FROM` — NEVER off the self-mutated state row, the supersede-double-count guard), (`grader_confidence = shadow.normalization_confidence × 1.0`, `parser_confidence` passed in from `done.py`). **§3 steps 1-3 — the SINGLE combined-likelihood update per entity (NOT a per-event chain):** events are GROUPED by `entity_id` and the §3 update is computed ONCE per group from the FROZEN WU-5A1 belief primitives — (step 1) multiply the per-event RAW `likelihood_for_event` vectors into ONE combined `L`, (step 2) `damp` the COMBINED `L` ONCE with `q = parser_confidence·grader_confidence`, (step 3) ONE `bayes_update` over the recompute base. This deliberately does NOT chain `apply_event`: the §3.1 affine damper `q·L+(1−q)·(1,1,1)` is NOT multiplicative-homomorphic, so `damp(L1)·damp(L2) ≠ damp(L1·L2)` for `q<1` — chaining (damp+renormalize per event) would diverge from the spec. For a single event the combined update is numerically identical to `apply_event` (so the common path is unchanged). An entity carrying >1 event in ONE Done (reachable today: a CONTRADICTION + a COVERED on the same `canonical_key` both surface as standalone events under the structurally-empty `opposes_map`) gets a SINGLE belief update. It appends one `MasteryEvent` per mapped event (the event log; the belief columns on each row record the single base→combined transition that actually occurred) but upserts `LearnerState` ONCE per entity with the combined posterior — `states_upserted` counts distinct entities, and evidence_count INCREMENTS once per Done (=1 on fresh insert) "fires once per Done episode, never per turn"; `last_evidence_at`/`updated_at` = `done_ts` (`prior_last_evidence_at`, read off the locked prior state, anchors only the recorded-not-applied `dt_days_since_last` — v1 applies NO decay, deferred to WU-5B). An abstained/empty conversion writes NOTHING → `LearnerUpdateResult(0, 0, (), abstained=True)`. `LearnerUpdateResult` is a frozen dataclass `(events_written, states_upserted, skipped_unmapped, abstained)`. Persistence + Done wiring are WU-5A2. **WU-5B1 adds `decay.py` — the PURE §3 Step-0 between-session decay (no IO; mirrors `belief.py` — `import math`, named constants, returns NEW tuples).** `DECAY_K=0.05` (half-life `ln2/k=13.86` d, LOCKED); `decay_weight(dt_days, k=DECAY_K) = 1−e^(−k·max(0,dt_days))` — the `max(0,·)` clamp kills negative-Δt sharpening (clock skew / out-of-order retry → w=0 → identity) and `dt=0` → w=0 → identity (no spurious same-day forgetting); `decay_toward_prior(belief, prior, dt_days, k=DECAY_K)` = the convex blend `(1−w)·belief + w·prior` toward `COLD_START_PRIOR` (passed IN, NEVER re-literal'd — every component ≥0.20>0 so the blend REPAIRS zeros and honors the §3 'never 0' invariant; a convex combination of two sum-1 vectors stays sum-1 with no renormalize). **The `prior_transform` injected seam + dt-hoist in `persistence.py` (additive, adjudication #1 — identity-default, every WU-5A2 test stays byte-identical green, the non-regression proof):** `_combined_belief_update` now computes `dt_days_since_last` at the TOP of the body (a PURE reordering — dt is a function of `done_ts`/`prior_last_evidence_at` only, both immutable+unmutated, and feeds the readout AND, when present, the Step-0 transform — so the VALUE is unchanged) and accepts a keyword-only `prior_transform: PriorTransform | None = None` (alias `Callable[[tuple[float,float,float], int|None], tuple[float,float,float]]`) threaded `persist_learner_update` → `_persist_entity_group` → `_combined_belief_update`; when provided it DECAYS the recompute-base prior (read off the EVENT LOG, NOT the state row) BEFORE damp/bayes, so `BeliefUpdate.prior_belief` then records the DECAYED prior (the intended §3 Step-0→Step-3 chain); default `None` skips the line → byte-identical to WU-5A2. **Decay is UPDATE-time, anchored to the frozen `done_ts` (never `now()`), INTEGER-day (`.days` truncation accepted, adjudication #3), clamped Δt≥0**, pulled toward `COLD_START_PRIOR`. It fires ONLY for an entity that RECEIVES an event this Done; the "unseen entity drifts to unknown" READ-TIME readout (§3 L415) is a PHASE-6 reader concern, explicitly NOT WU-5B1 (no `now()` anywhere on this path). `done.py` is UNCHANGED — the decay flag is read inside `learner_update.py`, so the `run_learner_update` call site stays byte-identical. No migration (`dt_days_since_last` already shipped + populated by WU-5A2). **WU-5B2 adds `negotiation.py` — the PURE §3 negotiation-move likelihood multiplier (the §3 L428 negotiation-move row `— / ×1.2 / ×1.1`) + one tiny async read (no Neo4j).** Constants: `NEGOTIATION_LIKELIHOOD=(1.0,1.2,1.1)` order `(p_misc,p_shaky,p_mastered)` — the blank `L_misc` cell is the identity 1.0 (L430 "never 0"), shaky/mastered boost; `MULTIPLIER_MOVES={challenge,paraphrase}` (`skip` / `None` / unknown → no-op `NO_OP_LIKELIHOOD` identity — adjudication #4); `STUDENT_ACTOR="student"` (the 021 CHECK allows student/parser/system; the store always writes `student`, so the read MUST filter it). Pure fns: `negotiation_multiplier(move)` → the LOCKED row or identity (never a 0 component); `entity_negotiation_move(entity_events, moves)` → the representative move = the move on the LAST (deterministic converter order) of the entity's `evidence_node_ids` that has a move (EXACTLY ONE per entity — a student spamming moves cannot stack/inflate); `suppresses_hedge(entity_events)` → the RATIFIED adjudication #4b: `True` on any MISCONCEPTION OR a PARTIAL-with-`misconception_code` (the ambiguous-order conflict event), `False` on CORRECTED (the student fixed it — boost ALLOWED) / plain COVERED / plain PARTIAL. The one IO read `load_student_moves(db, *, attempt_id) -> {entry_id: move}` selects `apollo_kg_negotiations` WHERE `attempt_id=:id AND actor='student'` ordered `(created_at ASC, id ASC)` so the LAST row per `entry_id` wins (latest-wins; the `id` tiebreak makes a same-instant `created_at` deterministic) — parser/system rows EXCLUDED, NO Neo4j (the KG bridge is the events' in-memory `evidence_node_ids`). **The additive `persistence.py` seam (identity-default, every WU-5A2/5B1 test stays byte-identical green with the flag OFF — the non-regression proof):** two keyword-only callables `likelihood_multiplier_for_entity(entity_events)` (→ a 3-tuple multiplier) + `negotiation_move_for_entity(entity_events)` (→ `str` or `None`) threaded `persist_learner_update` → `_persist_entity_group` → `_combined_belief_update`. `_persist_entity_group` resolves `entity_multiplier` (identity `NO_OP_LIKELIHOOD` when the callable is `None`) + `negotiation_move` (`None` when the callable is `None`), passes the multiplier into `_combined_belief_update` (which folds it into the COMBINED likelihood ONCE per entity AFTER the per-event product and BEFORE damp — so a low-q attempt MUTES the metacognitive bump; `q` stays `parser·grader`, the multiplier is NOT folded into `q`), and OVERRIDES the frozen `MasteryEventRowSpec.negotiation_move=None` at the ORM-build site via `dataclasses.replace(spec, negotiation_move=move)` (immutable, frozen-spec-safe — NOT by editing `update.py`/`state_model.py`). The two are DECOUPLED on purpose: suppression mutes the MULTIPLIER (identity) but the move STRING is persisted UNCONDITIONALLY (so the refit corpus can later re-fit the sign). Defaults (`None` callables → `NO_OP_LIKELIHOOD` multiply `a·1.0=a` + `replace(…,None)` no-op) → byte-identical to WU-5B1. **The locked vectors:** a misconception entity with a qualifying move is SUPPRESSED to identity (`p_misc=0.4839`, restoring the −0.044 cancel a literal multiply would dilute); a covered@0.6 q=0.7 entity boosts BEFORE-damp to mastery `0.5209` (distinct from the after-damp `0.5232` — proves the before-damp form). No migration (`negotiation_move` (026) + `apollo_kg_negotiations` (021) already exist). **WU-6A1 adds `personalization_read.py` — the FIRST read path over `apollo_learner_state` (the existing `_lock_prior_state` is a `FOR UPDATE` write-lock, NOT reused).** `read_learner_profile(db, *, user_id, search_space_id, concept_id) -> LearnerProfile` is a pure, no-lock, course-scoped read (≤3 scoped queries, no N+1, no `commit`/`flush`/mutation): it loads this concept's `apollo_kg_entities` (the id↔canonical_key maps), the learner's `apollo_learner_state` rows scoped by BOTH `user_id` AND `search_space_id` AND `entity_id IN (concept entities)` (the §1.4 per-classroom isolation invariant — mastery never crosses courses), and the WITHIN-CONCEPT `apollo_entity_prereqs` edges (BOTH endpoints among those entities, so `prereq_edges` is self-contained — every endpoint resolves through the id↔key maps; a cross-concept edge is excluded). It returns the frozen `LearnerProfile{by_canonical_key (raw `EntityProfile` columns — `mastery`/`confidence`/`misconception_code` read VERBATIM, NO `belief.py` recompute), prereq_edges (raw `(from,to)` tuples, deterministically sorted), entity_id_by_key, key_by_entity_id, is_empty}`. `is_empty=True` is the PROD cold-start path (`apollo_learner_state` is empty while `APOLLO_GRAPH_SIM_LAYER3_ENABLED` is OFF) — on cold-start the maps/edges still populate, only `by_canonical_key` is empty; an unknown concept (zero entities) short-circuits to a fully-empty profile before the state/prereq queries. It does NOT compute `prereqs_mastered` (that pure semantic + the band/threshold constants are WU-6A2's `personalization_select.py`) and imports NOTHING from a future `personalization_select` module (one-way dependency arrow, no cycle). No migration, no Neo4j, no LLM. Real-PG tested in `tests/database/test_personalization_read_postgres.py` (course-isolation, cold-start, column-read parity, prereq-edge + id↔key maps round-trip, cross-concept-edge exclusion, unknown-concept short-circuit, mixed present/absent, other-user filter). **WU-6A2 adds `personalization_select.py` — the PURE (no-IO) selection + coverage + difficulty algorithm** (mirrors `belief.py`; stdlib `set`/`dict`/`sorted` only, NO DB/LLM/Neo4j/container/migration). It CONSUMES the frozen WU-6A1 `LearnerProfile` + an in-memory candidate `Problem` pool and returns the `Problem` whose reference graph best covers the student's weak-and-teachable entities. NAMED constants (6A2 owns every number, orchestrator-adjudicated): `TEACHABLE_BAND_LO=0.3`/`TEACHABLE_BAND_HI=0.7` (the spec §6 L470 teachable band, inclusive), `MASTERED_THRESHOLD=0.7` (prereq-mastered cut), `UNSEEN_MASTERY=0.50` (an entity with no learner_state row), `REPROBE_CONFIDENCE=0.4` (low-confidence soft-hold). `reference_entity_keys(problem)` reconstructs each candidate's canonical-key set IN-MEMORY via the FROZEN `_ENTRY_TYPE_TO_KIND_PREFIX` (imported from `learner_model_seed`) — PROVEN identical to the seeded `canonical_key`s (3-way parity across all 5 seed problems), so there is NO per-problem DB/Neo4j round-trip (NO N+1; the parsed `Problem` drops the seeded `entity_key`). `prereqs_mastered(profile,key)` derives the prereq gate purely from 6A1's RAW `prereq_edges` (FROM-depends-on-TO) + id↔key maps — an UNSEEN prereq (0.50<0.70) BLOCKS (conservative). `weak_teachable(profile)` = present entities in `[0.3,0.7]` with mastered prereqs (deficit `1-mastery`; low confidence never excludes — soft re-probe). `coverage_score(problem,weak)` = deficit-weighted sum over covered weak entities. `personalize_selection(profile,pool,*,concept_id,difficulty,attempted_ids)` filters to the in-difficulty unattempted candidates (clamp-within-choice; anti-starvation filter preserved), raises the BYTE-IDENTICAL `PoolExhaustedError(concept_cluster_id=str(concept_id),difficulty=…)` when none remain, returns `candidates[0]` on a cold-start/empty-weak profile (the non-regression anchor == today's `select_problem`), else the max-coverage candidate, tie-break lowest `Problem.id` (made EXPLICIT, pool-order-independent). It imports NOTHING from 6A1 in reverse (one-way arrow, no cycle) and is NOT re-exported through the package root (`__init__.py` `__all__` stays the WU-5A1 set); WU-6A3 imports it by submodule path. Pure golden-vector tested in `apollo/learner_model/tests/test_personalization_select.py` (locked constants; 3-way round-trip parity on all 5 seed problems; the band/prereq/soft-hold predicates; deficit-weighted pick + lowest-id tie-break + cold-start fallback + `PoolExhaustedError` byte-identity + `standard` single-candidate degeneracy + attempted-ids filter). |
| `apollo/overseer/` | `coverage.py`, `rubric.py`, `topic_score.py`, `diagnostic.py`, `misconception.py`, `misconception_bank.py`, `concept_inference.py`, `problem_selector.py`, `personalization_flag.py`, `xp.py` | Grading and orchestration brain. `coverage` = LLM semantic diff student-vs-reference (the **D4 fix**, flag-gated on `detector_enabled()`: `_BATCH_BINARY_PROMPT` now states sign flips/direction reversals are NOT equivalent, and `_batch_binary_match` pre-gates every `equation`-type ref/student pair through `tiers._symbolic_equiv` — a pair that is not sign-exact is forced `covered=False` regardless of the LLM verdict; the LLM may still downgrade a sympy-equal pair, never upgrade a sign-flipped one; flag OFF is byte-identical to pre-D4); `rubric` = deterministic weighted grade (no LLM); `topic_score.py` (2026-07-10, workspace spec `2026-07-10-apollo-topic-score-design.md`, §2) = NEW pure module, `compute_topic_score(*, coverage, reference_nodes, centrality, detection_outcome) -> TopicScoreResult` — replaces the fixed-axis rubric view with a per-reference-node topic checklist (credit is `procedure_scores[node_id]` whenever present — the grader is the grade; `per_step` "covered" is a fallback ONLY for a node absent from `procedure_scores`, and otherwise decides binary status, not credit — 2026-07-11, see the intro section above; weight from `compute_centrality` floored at `CENTRALITY_W_MIN` and normalized to sum 1, dock from `detection_outcome.ledger_findings` deduped by `canonical_key`/signature at max confidence and clamped at `SEVERITY_CLAMP`, unmappable findings routed to a synthetic `_general` bucket); reuses `rubric.py::score_to_letter` for the band (no duplicated thresholds). 2026-07-10 (spec section 3): NOW WIRED end to end behind `APOLLO_TOPIC_SCORE_SERVED` (`misconception_detector/config.py::topic_score_served_enabled()`, default OFF). `compute_topic_score` is invoked ALWAYS in `done.py::handle_done` (flag-independent, soft-fail-wrapped via `_compute_topic_score_safe` -- any exception logs and proceeds with `topic_score=None`), reusing the misconception detector's own `compute_centrality` output when that stage ran, else computing it fresh. The result always reaches the canonical artifact's `scores.topic_score` block (`{score, letter, coverage_component, misconception_dock, topics: [...]}`, serialized by the shared `topic_score_serialize.py::serialize_topic_score`/`serialize_topics` -- the ONE serializer both `grading/artifact_build.py`'s `build_llm_artifact`/`build_graph_artifact` and the served payload use, so the three surfaces never drift). Serving is flag-gated: when ON and the compute succeeded, `done.py` builds a NEW `served_rubric` dict (`rubric` itself, and the copy `write_artifacts`/`attempt.diagnostic_report` receive, are never mutated) whose `overall` is replaced with `{score, letter}` from the topic score while the three legacy axis blocks pass through UNCHANGED (mid-deploy safety for older UI clients); `student_response["topics"]` is added as the serialized topic list. XP ordering: `served_rubric` is built BEFORE `compute_xp_earned`, so under the flag XP is earned against the topic score, not the axis blend. The diagnostic narrative (`overseer/diagnostic.py::generate_diagnostic`, new `topic_score` kwarg) switches to a ledger-grounded prompt (`overseer/topic_narrative.py::build_topic_narrative_prompt`, pure) ONLY when the flag is on and a topic_score is present -- it names every topic's status/credit and every misconception's evidence span + dock points, forbids claims outside that ledger, and uses `$...$`-only inline math; flag off (or no topic_score) leaves the axis-based prompt byte-identical to pre-spec behavior. `diagnostic` = LLM narration of the rubric verdict (does NOT re-grade); `concept_inference` = Hoot transcript → concept_id (chosen from the course's `apollo_concepts` candidate rows, threaded in by the handler); `problem_selector` = DB problem bank loader (`apollo_concept_problems` by `concept_id` + `difficulty`; async, no filesystem, no cluster map); `xp` = pure-function XP/levels; `misconception*` = embedding-matched misconception bank (pgvector 3072, migration 019; not wired into the v1 turn). **WU-6A3 — the session-personalization wedge (Phase 6) goes LIVE.** `personalization_flag.is_enabled()` mirrors `misconception.py` for `APOLLO_SESSION_PERSONALIZATION_ENABLED` (default OFF everywhere incl. prod). `problem_selector.select_problem_personalized(db, *, user_id, search_space_id, concept_id, difficulty, attempted_ids)` wraps the UNTOUCHED `select_problem`: FLAG-OFF (default/prod) delegates byte-identically (no profile read, no log); FLAG-ON reads the candidate pool once + the WU-6A1 `read_learner_profile` once at the selection seam (no N+1, no per-turn read), delegates scoring + the cold-start branch to the frozen WU-6A2 `personalize_selection`, and emits ONE `event=personalized_selection` observability log (the only runtime signal the wedge engaged vs degraded). **Double-gated** with `APOLLO_GRAPH_SIM_LAYER3_ENABLED`: even flag-ON is a no-op in prod until Layer-3 populates `apollo_learner_state` (empty → `is_empty` → cold-start `candidates[0]`, byte-identical to flag-OFF). BOTH live selection call-sites route through it — `hoot_bridge/session_init.py` (session start) and `handlers/next.py` (next problem) — so the wedge fires at session start, not just on advance. `PoolExhaustedError` is raised byte-identically, before the log. **WU-3B2a — `problem_selector.list_problems_for_concept` is now Tier-2-gated:** the loader adds ONE `ConceptProblem.tier == 2` predicate so only teachable problems are returned — Tier-1 (auto-provisioned inventory, migration 030) is excluded. Because `list_problems_for_concept` is the SOLE chokepoint, this single predicate gates BOTH `select_problem` and `select_problem_personalized` with no separate edit. The seeded curriculum is teachable, so the migration's backfill flips existing `tier=1` rows to `tier=2` and the test seed-helper `seed_problems(..., tier=2)` mirrors that (the live bernoulli pool stays selectable). **WU-3B2h — the selectability gate is now `tier == 2 AND quarantined_at IS NULL`:** `list_problems_for_concept` adds the second `ConceptProblem.quarantined_at.is_(None)` predicate (mutation-proven: dropping it makes a quarantined problem selectable → the selector-exclusion test REDs). Because `list_problems_for_concept` is the SOLE chokepoint, this single predicate gates BOTH `select_problem` and `select_problem_personalized` with no separate edit and NO signature change; a quarantined problem (stamped by the `apollo.provisioning.quarantine` sweep) silently never appears in selection, and clearing `quarantined_at` makes it selectable again (reversible). **§9 SPEC-4 — the shadow invariant (the spec-closing test):** with `APOLLO_GRAPH_SIM_SHADOW_ENABLED` ON + `APOLLO_GRAPH_SIM_LAYER3_ENABLED` OFF, an auto-provisioned-shaped Tier-2 problem is teachable (returns an OLD-path rubric/coverage/xp_earned grade, `result='graded'`, `learner_update_pending=False`), produces `apollo_graph_comparison_findings` (the data source the quarantine sweep consumes), AND moves ZERO Layer-3 beliefs (`apollo_mastery_events` + `apollo_learner_state` UNCHANGED) — proven verbatim by `tests/database/test_apollo_quarantine_shadow.py`. NOTE: in the v1 shadow path the persisted findings carry `entity_id=NULL` (the canonical_key→id join is a later concern) and the missing reference node's identity in `reference_node_ids`. The sweep keys its per-node aggregation on `reference_node_ids` PRECISELY for this reason, so these production findings DO drive the per-node concentration — the `test_shadow_findings_feed_sweep_end_to_end` BRIDGE runs the real shadow `handle_done` and then `sweep_quarantine` over its emitted findings, proving the two deliverables compose end-to-end (keying on the always-NULL `entity_id` would make quarantine inert against real data — the bridge REDs under that mutation). The Layer-2 sweep tests additionally hand-write `reference_node_ids` findings to exercise the concentration/reversibility/scoping branches. The auto-provisioning substrate (the five new tables + the pipeline) lands in 3B2b–3B2h. **`apollo/overseer/misconception_detector/` (T1–T17, DEFAULT OFF) is a SEPARATE new package** — do not confuse it with the dormant `misconception.py`/`misconception_bank.py` pgvector matcher above (which stays unwired into the v1 turn). It is a parallel Done-time detection stage gated by `APOLLO_MISCONCEPTION_DETECTOR` (`config.py::detector_enabled()`, default OFF everywhere): `types.py` (frozen VOs — `ConceptFinding`/`DetectionResult`/`MergeOutcome`/`JudgeRaw`/`JudgeFn`/`EmbedFn` protocols), `centrality.py` (pure reference-graph centrality, PRECEDES-cycle-safe per A6), `sympy_veto.py` (deterministic Tier-1 sign/direction-mutant veto reusing `apollo.resolution.tiers._symbolic_equiv`), `bank_pattern.py` (Tier-1 embedding match against the SAME `apollo_misconceptions` bank via `misconception_bank`, DI'd `EmbedFn`; REDESIGNED 2026-07-08, A10 — now emits its best-ranked match even when BELOW `BANK_SIM_FLOOR`, tagged `bank_match_above_floor=False`, so `gate.py` can use it as a floor-free corroboration witness for a co-keyed judge finding; `BANK_SIM_FLOOR` still gates whether the SAME match is standalone-dock-eligible, which it never is on its own regardless — a lone bank finding always drops at the gate), `judge.py` (Tier-2 comparative LLM judge behind the `JudgeFn` Protocol; `make_openai_judge` is the one live call site, using `client.chat.completions.create(..., logprobs=True, top_logprobs=5)` directly — NOT `agent._llm.main_chat` — to recover `verdict_token_prob`; REDESIGNED 2026-07-08, A11 — the forced JSON schema gains a required `misconception_code` string per concept row; `_finding_from_row` validates the named code against THAT concept's own `bank_entries` (never a global code set) and keys `bank_code`/`signature=misc.<code>` only on an exact match, else stays `unkeyed:<concept_key>` — a hallucinated/empty/cross-concept/absent code degrades gracefully, never raises), `gate.py` (corroboration + dual-τ gate, REDESIGNED 2026-07-08 — A9-A13 "judge-authoritative gate": `sympy_veto` self-docks and is always ceiling-eligible; a `judge` finding that names a `misconception_code` VALIDATED against the concept's own bank (`judge.py`, A11) is bank-keyed (`bank_code`/`misc.<code>` signature) and, if a `bank_pattern` finding ANYWHERE in the detection result shares that SAME validated `bank_code` (floor-free — `BANK_SIM_FLOOR` no longer gates corroboration, A10), docks under the JUDGE finding (ceiling-eligible); a LONE bank-keyed judge clearing BOTH its routed τ and the stricter `TAU_SOLO_JUDGE` may dock on its own but is penalty-only, NEVER ceiling-eligible (A9/A12 — one uncorroborated LLM opinion subtracts but cannot cap the band); a lone UNKEYED judge or a keyed-but-sub-solo-τ judge routes to `needs_clarification`; a lone `bank_pattern` finding (no judge ever names its code) never docks. **A13 cross-namespace fix:** the judge tier keys findings by the reference-graph node's `node_id`, but `bank_pattern` keys by the SESSION-scoped `str(concept_id)` — a different namespace AND cardinality — so `gate_findings` co-keys corroboration on the validated `bank_code` via a `bank_by_code` index (NOT `concept_key` equality), and the docked representative of any bank-corroborated dock is ALWAYS the judge/sympy finding (node_id-keyed, so `centrality.py`'s node_id-keyed map resolves it), never the bank witness. Both dock/clarify builders use `dataclasses.replace` so `bank_code`/`bank_match_above_floor`/`ceiling_eligible` are never silently dropped from a docked row), `merge.py` (severity = centrality × confidence, Σ clamped at `SEVERITY_CLAMP`, anti-dilution ceiling → `MergeOutcome` — `ceiling_applied` now reads the gate-stamped `ceiling_eligible` bit per docked finding, NOT centrality alone, so a penalty-only lone-judge dock can subtract without ever tripping the ceiling, A12), `detector.py` (`detect_misconceptions(...)` orchestrator — parallel tiers, judge/embed DI, any tier exception soft-fails to zero findings from that tier), and `apply.py` (pure `MergeOutcome` → penalized composite/rubric via `apply_penalty`/`rubric_overall_after_penalty`, replicating the inline `round(max(0.0,min(1.0,x)),6)` rather than importing the private `_round_like_composite`, A8). **`trace.py` (Phase-1 diagnostic, DEFAULT OFF via a SEPARATE flag `APOLLO_MISC_TRACE`, `config.py::trace_enabled()`):** instrumentation-only — it changes NO tau/gate row/threshold/scoring. When ON it re-derives, per reference-graph concept node, READ-ONLY from the same artifacts the live chain already produced (`DetectionResult` + `gate_findings` output + `MergeOutcome` + centrality map + reference graph), one machine-parseable JSONL row capturing what the judge said (`verdict`/`misconception_code`/`confidence`/`verdict_token_prob_present`), the finding `signature`/`bank_code`, the below-floor `bank_pattern` top-1 (code + similarity + above_floor), the gate decision (`dock`/`needs_clarification`/`drop`) and WHICH §5 row fired (co-key row 3 / lone-solo row 5 / row 6/7/8 / sympy row 1_2 / no_judge), the node's centrality, and the per-attempt roll-up (final band + `is_false_strong`). Rows append to `config.trace_path()` (`APOLLO_MISC_TRACE_PATH`, default `campaign/out/misconception_trace.jsonl`); the emit soft-fails. Wired at TWO seams behind the flag: `done.py`'s detector block (its OWN try/except so a trace defect never perturbs the already-computed grade; `is_control=False`, `final_band` = the letter rubric band) and `campaign/validate_misconception_detector.py` (which supplies the labeled `is_control` + the scorecard band, so its `is_false_strong` is the real residual false-Strong roll-up the recall gap targets). Flag OFF ⇒ `trace.py` is never imported and behaviour/output is byte-identical. See `## Main data flows (b)` step 5a for the Done-time wiring and the `APOLLO_EMERGENT_MISCONCEPTIONS` interaction. **F-struct — structural co-key (2026-07-09, SEPARATE sub-flag `APOLLO_MISC_STRUCT_COKEY`, `config.py::struct_cokey_enabled()`, default OFF, only meaningful when `APOLLO_MISCONCEPTION_DETECTOR` is also ON):** closes the recall gap where a judge LOCALIZES an error to a reference node (`wrong`/`misconception` verdict, routed-τ clears) but names no validated `misconception_code` — previously this always fell through to `needs_clarification`/drop even when the CURRICULUM ALREADY KNOWS the opposing misconception for that concept. Two new authored-data seams make this resolvable: every `Node` gains an optional `entity_key: str | None` field (the authoring name for the concept it represents, e.g. `"def.real_basis"`, populated on reference nodes built from the problem's declared paths — orthogonal to `node_id`, which stays the per-attempt graph key) and `apollo_misconceptions` gains an `opposes: str | None` column (migration 039) naming the `entity_key` of the concept a bank entry corrects a wrong belief about, backfilled from `misconceptions.json`'s existing `opposes` authoring field (`apollo/overseer/misconception_bank.py::MisconceptionEntry.opposes`). `opposes_index.py::build_opposes_index(reference_graph, bank_entries) -> dict[str, str]` (pure, no IO) is the resolver seam: for every bank entry with a non-None `opposes`, it looks up the reference node whose `entity_key` matches and maps that node's `node_id -> bank_code` (D3: on a multi-opposes tie the lexicographically-lowest code wins) — this is a `node_id`-keyed map, NOT `entity_key`-keyed, so it lines up exactly with `gate.py`'s own `concept_key` (== `node_id`) keying and `centrality.py`'s node_id-keyed map. `gate_findings`'s `_gate_one_concept` consumes it in a NEW branch reached ONLY when the best judge finding is unkeyed (`bank_code is None`, no bank corroboration): if `opposes_index.get(concept_key)` hits AND the judge clears its routed τ AND its verdict is `wrong`/`misconception`, `_struct_docked` builds the docked representative via `dataclasses.replace` (verdict forced to `misconception`, `corroborated=True`, `ceiling_eligible=True`, `bank_code`/`signature=misc.<code>` set to the graph-named code) — reusing the existing row-3 co-key shape so `merge.py` needs no change to emit the artifact `misconceptions[]` row. Wired in `done.py`'s T13 detector block: `opposes_index` defaults to `{}`; when the sub-flag is ON, `_load_bank_entries` (a small soft-failing local mirror of `detector._load_bank` — DB error or no `concept_id` degrades to an empty bank, never raises) loads the concept's bank and `build_opposes_index(reference_graph, bank_entries)` builds the real map, passed to BOTH `gate_findings(detection.per_concept, opposes_index=opposes_index)` and (when `APOLLO_MISC_TRACE` is also ON) `trace_attempt(..., opposes_index=opposes_index)` — the SAME map object, so the trace's structural-dock label matches the real gate decision it observed. Sub-flag OFF (default, prod) -> `opposes_index` stays `{}`, `build_opposes_index` is never even imported, and `gate_findings`/`trace_attempt` see the exact empty-map default they always had — byte-identical. `trace.py` extends its per-node JSONL row with `struct_opposes_code` (the `opposes_index` lookup for that node, `None` if none), `docked_via` (`"struct_opposes"` / `"judge_named"` / `"sympy"` / `"none"` — which of the three real dock kinds fired, or none), and the row label gains `"row3s_struct_cokey_dock"` alongside the existing §5 truth-table rows — all read-only re-derivations that never perturb the actual gate/merge decision. **Grader positive-focus (2026-07-10 design `docs/_archive/specs/2026-07-10-grader-positive-focus-design.md`, T-W5a) — new flag `APOLLO_GRADER_POSITIVE_FOCUS` (`config.py::grader_positive_focus_enabled()`, default OFF):** neutralizes the coverage/rubric grader's wrongness-sensitivity so the detector/emergent-map channel is the sole penalty authority, at four sites (P1–P4) all fed by the one `detection_outcome` computed once in `done.py`. P1 (`done.py`, `rubric_overall_after_penalty` call) — SKIPPED when ON: the served rubric/band/XP become credit-only, while `detection_outcome` is still threaded to `write_artifacts` so `misconceptions[]` feedback fidelity is unchanged. P2 (`apollo/grading/artifact_build.py`'s `apply_penalty` call in `build_llm_artifact`) — RETAINED unconditionally as the sole penalty channel when the flag is ON (deliberate design choice; a P2-also-off variant was explicitly not built — future option only if requested). P3 (`apollo/overseer/coverage.py`'s `_sign_gate_equation_verdicts`) — SKIPPED when ON: a sign-reversed equation stays coverage-credited, and the detector still names the wrongness in the feedback channel. P4 (`done.py`'s `_attempt_misconception_scores` feeding this module's `compute_rubric` axis) — filtered to resolved-only (score ≥ 1.0) contributions when ON, dropping unresolved (0.5) drag — credit-only. Flag OFF (default): all four paths byte-identical to pre-branch. A promoted (τ_assert) emergent misconception feeds the SAME `detection_outcome`/`MergeOutcome` channel as an authored one — positive-focus does not gate the emergent map itself, only which served surface (P1 rubric band vs P2 composite) the resulting penalty touches. |
| `apollo/emergent/` | `config.py`, `trust.py`, `store.py`, `capture.py`, `materialize.py` | **Emergent per-class misconception store (memo `docs/_archive/specs/2026-07-05-emergent-misconception-store-design.md`, increment 1; lane B3b/D1).** DORMANT behind `APOLLO_EMERGENT_MISCONCEPTIONS` (default OFF): flag OFF ⇒ grading output byte-identical to the hand-authored-bank-only behavior, zero ledger rows written. `config` = the flag + the OQ2 trust-gradient constants (K=3, τ_assert=0.5, τ_project=0.2, recency half-life 30d — all env-overridable, PRE-CALIBRATION). `trust` = PURE trust math: `trust = min(1, distinct_students/K)·mean_confidence·recency_factor` (exponential half-life decay), with `band` labels over thresholds (candidate/observed/promoted — NOT a stored `approved` bit) and the `unkeyed:*` bucket that never promotes. `store` = write seam `record_observations_from_canonical` (derives one idempotent observation per `(attempt, signature)` from a `role='canonical'` artifact's `misconceptions[]`/`node_ledger[]`, `ON CONFLICT (attempt_id, signature) DO NOTHING`) + derived-on-read `aggregate_signatures` / `load_class_misconceptions` / `load_promoted_misconceptions_dict` (nothing is materialized — increment 2 defers the rolled-up bank + teacher curation). Wired at TWO seams, both flag-gated: `handlers/artifact_writer.write_artifacts` (write, after the canonical commit, own failure domain) and `clarification/candidate_assembly.load_problem_candidates_with_soundness` (read — promoted emergent misconceptions become `misc.*` candidates exactly like bank entries; hand-authored keys WIN a collision). Table `apollo_misconception_observations`, migration 037. **Increment 2 — the emergent MAP (2026-07-10 design, `docs/_archive/specs/2026-07-10-emergent-misconception-map-design.md`; see "Non-obvious conventions" below for the full loop).** `capture.py` = `record_detector_births` / `record_clarification_refuted`, the two write helpers over `store.record_observation` for the new `source='detector_unkeyed'`/`'clarification_refuted'` seams. `materialize.py` = `materialize_if_promotable`, eager τ_project upsert-to-`:Canon`. Two NEW independent flags, both default OFF: `APOLLO_EMERGENT_MAP_CAPTURE` (`config.py::emergent_map_capture_enabled()`) and `APOLLO_EMERGENT_MAP_ASSERT` (`config.py::emergent_map_assert_enabled()`) — the legacy `APOLLO_EMERGENT_MISCONCEPTIONS` flag above is UNCHANGED in meaning but its scope NARROWED to gate only the increment-1 `record_observations_from_canonical` feed; the promoted-emergent grade-read in `candidate_assembly.py` now requires `APOLLO_EMERGENT_MAP_ASSERT` explicitly. Migration 040 adds a CHECK constraint enumerating `apollo_misconception_observations.source` to `('grading_artifact', 'detector_unkeyed', 'clarification_refuted')`; NOT applied to any remote Supabase project (local-Docker-only per this repo's DB contract — test rehearsal then prod is a human/CI step). |
| `apollo/solver/` | `sympy_exec.py`, `forward_chain.py`, `sufficiency.py`, `narrator.py` | SymPy forward-chaining solver + per-turn sufficiency signal. **Unwired in v1** — `done.py` sets `attempt.solver_trace = None` and never calls it; `sympy_exec.parse_zero_form` is still used by `store.py` for best-effort LaTeX rendering of equation nodes. |
| `apollo/agent/` | `apollo_llm.py`, `_llm.py`, `output_filter.py`, `leakage_judge.py` | `apollo_llm.draft_reply()` = the confused-learner reply (temp 0.7, strict ignorance prompt, 100k-token budget → `ContextOverflowError`). `_llm.py` = shared `cheap_chat`/`main_chat` helpers with per-call audit logging. `output_filter` + `leakage_judge` = two-stage anti-leak filter; `output_filter` is **unwired in v1** (replaced by structural isolation; see conventions); `leakage_judge` is now **WIRED** as the clarification-reply backstop (`guard_clarification_reply` in `apollo/clarification/leak_guard.py`, soft-fail-open) as of the clarification loop — it runs the judge callable directly (NOT the raising `validate_or_raise`) over any reply that carried probe hints, and re-drafts without probes on a confident leak (confidence ≥ `CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD` 0.6). |
| `apollo/persistence/` | `models.py`, `neo4j_client.py`, `progress_repo.py`, `attempt_history.py`, `learner_model_seed.py`, `misconception_bank_seed.py` | SQLAlchemy models for all `apollo_*` Postgres tables — including the WU-3A learner-model models `KGEntity`, `EntityPrereq`, `LearnerState`, `MasteryEvent`, `GraphComparisonRun`, `GraphComparisonFinding` (migration 026) plus the allowlist constants `ENTITY_KINDS` (mirrors the `apollo_kg_entities.kind` CHECK), `MASTERY_EVENT_KINDS`/`FINDING_KINDS` (open enums, documentation only), and the `Subject.search_space_id` (course-scoping, NOT NULL) / `ProblemAttempt.learner_update_pending` (§6/§7 retry flag) additions; **WU-5B3a-0 (migration 028)** adds five more `ProblemAttempt` columns — `apollo_problem_attempts.learner_update_{attempts,failed_at,last_error,next_attempt_at,failed_permanently}` (dead-letter + exponential-backoff bookkeeping for the learner_update retry janitor; INTEGER + BOOLEAN carry `server_default`, the three TIMESTAMPTZ/TEXT are nullable) + the partial index `apollo_problem_attempts_pending_idx ON (created_at) WHERE learner_update_pending AND NOT learner_update_failed_permanently`. WU-5B3a-0 ships the DDL + ORM mapping ONLY; the drain state machine (WU-5B3a-1) consumes them. NO `graded_at` column — the `done_ts` lives on the Neo4j nodes (`stamp_graded_at` / `read_node_graded_at`). async Neo4j driver wrapper (env-only credentials); XP repo (`load_progress`/`apply_xp`); cross-session re-attempt detection. `learner_model_seed.py` is the **WU-3B pure conversion core** (no SQLAlchemy import, so the fast tests need no DB): deterministic, LLM-free functions that turn the bernoulli source files into migration-026 Layer-1 row specs — `concept_dag_to_entities`/`concept_dag_to_prereqs` (14 concept entities + 16 prereq pairs), `symbols_to_entities` (7 canonical + `var.q` so the dynamic-pressure normalization alias is not lost; all 23 mappings placed as aliases), `reference_solution_to_entities` (equation→`eq.`/condition→`cond.`/simplification→`condition` `simp.`/procedure_step→`proc.`; **WU-3B2d additively extends `_ENTRY_TYPE_TO_KIND_PREFIX` with `variable_mapping → (variable, varmap)`** so a §8B auto-provisioned problem carrying a `variable_mapping` step mints (no `KeyError`) and 3B2b's gate-1 mint-map membership sub-check ACCEPTS it instead of failing CLOSED — additive only; no seeded problem uses `variable_mapping`, so the WU-6A2 `reference_entity_keys` golden vectors are byte-identical, proven by the `test_personalization_select` anchor staying green), `misconceptions_to_entities` (carrying `opposes_entity_key`), `authored_definitions` (backward-compatible bernoulli entry point; returns the single `def.pressure_velocity_tradeoff` which is not a reference-solution node), **`authored_definitions_from_spec(entries)`** (generalized: converts a concept's optional `authored_definitions.json` dicts into `definition` EntitySpecs — used when a misconception opposes a non-reference key; not needed for macro concepts whose misconceptions oppose real reference nodes), the immutable `annotate_reference_solution` (adds `entity_key` per step + `declared_paths` + `layer1_seeded`), and **`validate_reference_graph`** — the executable §6.1 reference-graph validation contract WU-4A consumes (every reference node must carry an entity link AND a non-empty declared path covering every node, else grading is blocked). The DB write layer that calls these lives in `scripts/seed_apollo_learner_model.py` (see `domain-data.md`). **WU-3A is schema + ORM ONLY**; **WU-3B is the data fixture** (Layer-1 rows + reference-solution links); **WU-3C1 is the `:Canon` projection** (`scripts/seed_canon_projection.py` rebuild CLI → `knowledge_graph/canon_projection.py`). `neo4j_schema.cypher` (the prod/Aura schema authority, applied once on the instance) gains the WU-3C1 `:Canon(key)` uniqueness constraint (`canon_key_unique`, the upsert/no-duplicate enforcer behind the application `MERGE`) plus `:Canon(search_space_id)` and `:_KGNode(user_id)` indexes (the existing `:_KGNode(attempt_id)` index stays). Still later: the §5 resolver (`RESOLVES_TO` edges + resolution fields — WU-3C2), the §3 belief-update math, the §6 grading core, and the §8A runtime cutover (WU-3D). Following the repo convention, these ORM models declare **no DB CHECK constraints** — migration 026 SQL is the authority; the `user_id → auth.users` FK lives only in the migration (auth.users is Supabase-managed, not in `Base.metadata`). **WU-3B2a (migration 030 §8B auto-provisioning substrate — schema + ORM + the Tier-2 gate only, NO pipeline/LLM logic)** adds five `ConceptProblem` columns — `tier` (`SmallInteger`, SQL `server_default=1` / ORM `default=2` because authored curriculum is teachable; the `CHECK (tier IN (1,2))` lives in SQL), `solution_source`, `provenance` (`_JSONType` default `{}`), `quarantined_at` (nullable; its selector filter is WU-3B2h's, NOT added now), and `search_space_id` (nullable denormalized course scope, no ORM FK) — one `KGEntity.scope_summary` column (nullable; the dedup ladder's embedding source, embedded on the fly by 3B2c), and **five new model classes** mirroring the new course-scoped tables: `IngestRun` (`apollo_ingest_runs` — per-doc run counts + LLM call/token/cost aggregates; `status` queued/running/succeeded/failed), `ProvisioningJob` (`apollo_provisioning_jobs` — the SKIP-LOCKED queue, `state` pending/running/completed/failed; the partial-unique-index that collapses two OPEN jobs per document is migration-only, NOT in the ORM), `RejectedProblem`, `DedupDecision` (`similarity` REAL/`Float`; `method` slug/embedding/llm_judge, `verdict` merged/distinct), and `IngestError`.
