Every new class carries `search_space_id` (`Integer` FK `aita_search_spaces` ON DELETE CASCADE — the §1.4 isolation invariant) and declares no DB CHECK (SQL is the authority); ORM round-trips are guarded by `apollo/persistence/tests/test_autoprovisioning_models.py` (real PG) and the DDL by `tests/database/test_apollo_autoprovisioning_migration.py`. **Migration 034 (canonical grading artifact, campaign-plan Task A1)** adds `GradingArtifact` (`apollo_grading_artifacts`) — ONE immutable row per Done-click per grader `role` (`canonical` = what the student was served, `pair` = the other grader's artifact captured on the same input, UNIQUE `(attempt_id, role)`), `grader_used` (`graph`/`llm_fallback`), FKs `attempt_id → apollo_problem_attempts` CASCADE / `search_space_id → aita_search_spaces` CASCADE / `concept_id → apollo_concepts` SET NULL (mirrors `Clarification.concept_id` exactly), plus JSONB `versions`/`node_ledger`/`edge_ledger`/`misconceptions`/`clarification_trace`/`scores`/`abstention` and `grading_latency_ms`. Following repo convention the ORM declares no `role`/`grader_used` CHECK (SQL migration is the authority — verified for real by `tests/database/test_apollo_grading_artifacts_constraints.py`, which applies migration 034 verbatim to a scratch DB on the session pgvector container, mirroring `test_apollo_attempt_result_constraint.py`); the ORM-visible UNIQUE constraint and JSON round-trip are covered by `tests/database/test_apollo_grading_artifacts_migration.py` via the standard `db_session`/`Base.metadata.create_all` harness. LOCAL-Docker-verified only — migration 034 is NOT applied to any remote Supabase project. **`misconception_bank_seed.py` (2026-07-02, campaign-harness F1 defect fix)** is the pure conversion core for the OTHER misconception store — `apollo_misconceptions` (migration 019), the runtime misconception-inference bank + graph-grader soundness-axis input (`overseer/misconception_bank.py`), which is DISTINCT from `learner_model_seed.py`'s `kind='misconception'` `apollo_kg_entities` rows. Before this fix `apollo_misconceptions` had NO seeder anywhere in the repo (`upsert_entry`'s own docstring claimed "used by the seeder script", but none existed) — every campaign attempt aborted the shadow grader with `misconception_bank_empty`. `misconceptions_json_to_bank_specs(misc: dict) -> list[MisconceptionBankSpec]` derives the table's authoring-specific fields (`code` from `key` minus the `misc.` prefix, a generated Socratic `probe_question` fallback when the source has none, optional `confusion_pair`/`rt_steps`) from the SAME `misconceptions.json` the KG-entity converter already reads — no new authoring format. DB-free; the write layer (`scripts/seed_apollo_misconceptions.py`) calls `overseer.misconception_bank.upsert_entry` per spec, embedding `description` via `embed_text` unless `--no-embeddings`. Wired into `campaign.cast.teacher.provision_seeded` as a new step between `seed_apollo_learner_model` and `seed_canon_projection`, so both campaign seeded incumbents (fluid_mechanics, macroeconomics) get a real bank. The WU-AAS authored path (`linear_motion`, `tag_and_mint`) has NO on-disk `misconceptions.json` and mints only `kind='misconception'` KG entities (never `apollo_misconceptions` rows, per the existing ADJ #2 deviation) — an authored subject's bank stays empty by design; `grade.soundness_applicable=False` (D5/D6 coverage-only fallback) is the correct, not-a-bug outcome there, not something this fix papers over. |

| `apollo/projections/` | `scorecard.py`, `mastery.py`, `classroom.py` | **Task B1** — read-side projections over the canonical grading artifact (campaign spec `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-07-01-system-scores-outputs-design.md` §2). `render_scorecard(artifact: dict) -> dict` is a PURE TEMPLATE over an already-built artifact payload dict (`apollo.grading.artifact_build.build_graph_artifact`/`build_llm_artifact` shape, or the identical JSONB-column shape of a persisted `GradingArtifact` row) — no DB/Neo4j/LLM calls, no recomputation. Maps `scores.composite` to 4 bands (`Strong`≥`APOLLO_BAND_STRONG` default 0.85 / `Proficient`≥`APOLLO_BAND_PROFICIENT` default 0.70 / `Developing`≥`APOLLO_BAND_DEVELOPING` default 0.50 / `Beginning` otherwise, via `load_bands()`, env read fresh every call like `composite.load_weights`) and reshapes the artifact's `node_ledger`/`misconceptions`/`clarification_trace` straight into `{score_0_100, band, taught_well: [{key, evidence_span}], missing_or_unclear: [{key, guidance}], watch_out: [{key, quote}], clarifications: [{question, answer, credit}]}`. `taught_well` = `credited` node-ledger rows verbatim, BUT the `evidence_span` key is emitted ONLY when a real non-empty span exists — a credited row with no span (`None` on the LLM-fallback path, which carries no per-node student utterance; or an edge-case `""`) renders as `{key}` WITHOUT the key, never as a fake empty quote (Q2/lane B4 fix, 2026-07-02 campaign: the block's purpose is "in the student's own words", so a blank quote is worse than an absent one; this eliminated the `evidence_span: ""` that rendered in all 12 F1c adjudication packets); `missing_or_unclear` = `unresolved` rows phrased via the fixed template `f"Next time, explain {key}"` (no generation); `watch_out` = the artifact's `misconceptions` block (evidence span as the quote); both graders' artifacts render through this identical template (same scorecard shape regardless of `grader_used`, spec §3 step 3). Wired into `done.py`'s Task A3 artifact-capture block (behind `APOLLO_GRADING_ARTIFACT_ENABLED`): `write_artifacts` now RETURNS the canonical payload dict it just persisted so `handle_done` can call `render_scorecard` on it directly and attach the additive `student_response["scorecard"]` key — `None` (artifact write failed, its own swallowed-exception failure domain) means no scorecard is attached rather than templating over a payload that never reached disk. **Task B2** — `mastery.py`'s `update_mastery_from_artifact(db, *, artifact_row: GradingArtifact) -> None` is the "mastery ledger only" projection (spec §2 Q3, "each artifact appends a mastery_event and updates learner_state per concept ... EWMA-style"): a SEPARATE, simpler write path from the dormant WU-5A2 Bayesian `run_learner_update` — never both active for the same attempt (guarded in `done.py`, see the `apollo/handlers/` row). Granularity note: the plan text says "per concept" but the reused `apollo_mastery_events`/`apollo_learner_state` columns are keyed by `entity_id` (one level below `GradingArtifact.concept_id`), so this projection writes one event/state row per DISTINCT resolvable `canonical_key` in the artifact's `node_ledger` (`credited`/`misconception` rows only; `unresolved` rows carry no entity-mappable key), resolved via the SAME `canon_projection.load_entity_specs(db, concept_id=...)` lookup WU-5A already uses (no new inference) — every touched entity gets the SAME artifact-level `scores.composite` as its evidence (v1 has no finer per-node score). `mastery = alpha*composite + (1-alpha)*prior_mastery` (`ewma_mastery`, clamped `[0,1]`; `alpha` = env `APOLLO_MASTERY_EWMA_ALPHA` default `0.3`, read fresh via `ewma_alpha()`); cold start (no prior `LearnerState` row) sets `prior_mastery = composite`, so a first-ever attempt's mastery is the composite itself for any alpha. `confidence` = the artifact's `abstention.normalization_confidence`, defaulting to `1.0` when absent (the LLM-fallback path records no such signal). The shared `belief` columns are re-encoded as `(1-mastery, 0.0, mastery)` so `apollo.learner_model.belief.mastery_of(belief) == mastery` exactly (no shaky-state signal in this projection). Idempotent per attempt via the existing `UNIQUE(attempt_id, entity_id, event_kind)` constraint with a distinct `event_kind="composite"` (never collides with WU-5A's `covered`/`missing`/`partial`/`misconception`/`corrected` kinds): a retry checks for an existing `(attempt_id, entity_id, "composite")` event first and skips that entity entirely when found. FLUSH-ONLY (mirrors `persist_learner_update`'s contract) — `done.py`'s `_project_mastery` owns the commit/rollback boundary. A no-op when `artifact_row.concept_id is None` or the ledger names no credited/misconception key. **Task B3** — `classroom.py`'s `mastery_heatmap(db, *, search_space_id) -> list[dict]` and `struggle_signals(db, *, search_space_id, window_days=DEFAULT_WINDOW_DAYS=14) -> dict` are the "classroom (heatmap + struggle signals)" projection (spec §2): pure read-side SQL, no new inference. `mastery_heatmap` joins `apollo_learner_state` to `apollo_kg_entities` (for the `entity_id -> concept_id` step-up — `LearnerState` is one level below the concept the heatmap groups by) and averages `mastery`/`confidence` across every entity under a concept into one `{user_id, concept_id, mastery, confidence}` cell per (user, concept); leverages the new migration-035 `ix_apollo_learner_state_space_entity (search_space_id, entity_id)` index (`apollo_learner_state`'s PK leads with `user_id`, so a course-wide scan can't use it). `struggle_signals` scans `apollo_grading_artifacts` rows created within the trailing window (review fix, Task B3 — no single `role` filter up front; each signal states its own row shape, since `build_llm_artifact` hardcodes `abstention.abstained = None` and an abstained shadow always serves the LLM grade as `role='canonical'`, pushing the abstained GRAPH artifact to `role='pair'`): `abstention_count` counts `grader_used='graph'` rows (any role) with `abstention->>'abstained' = 'true'` — scoping to `role='canonical'` here is structurally dead, since a promoted non-abstained graph grade is the only `role='canonical'`+`grader_used='graph'` combination and it can never be abstained; `fallback_count` counts `role='canonical'` `grader_used='llm_fallback'` rows that have a sibling `role='pair'` `grader_used='graph'` row for the same `attempt_id` (a REAL fallback from a graph attempt — not merely "the shadow chain never ran", which also serves `llm_fallback` with no graph row at all and must not count); `lowest_coverage_nodes` (per reference `canonical_key`, over `role='canonical'` rows, the credited-vs-not ratio via a `jsonb_array_elements(node_ledger)` lateral expansion filtered to `status IN ('credited','misconception')` OR (`status='unresolved'` AND `evidence_span IS NULL`) — the latter is a `_missing_ledger_entry` MISSING_NODE row (a real reference key, never taught) contributing 0.0 coverage — and, as of the Q2/lane B4 fix, ALSO an LLM-fallback `unresolved` row (`build_llm_artifact` now emits `evidence_span=None`, reference-keyed off `per_step`), so a concept the student didn't cover on an LLM-graded attempt now correctly surfaces as 0.0 coverage instead of being wrongly excluded by its old non-null `""`; a graph-path student-node-id-keyed `UNRESOLVED`-utterance `unresolved` row (`apollo.grading.artifact_build._unresolved_ledger_entry`) still carries a non-null `evidence_span` `""` and stays EXCLUDED), and `top_misconceptions` (count per `canonical_key` via `jsonb_array_elements(misconceptions)`, over `role='canonical'` rows); leverages `ix_grading_artifacts_space_concept_time (search_space_id, concept_id, created_at)` (migration 034) for the `search_space_id` equality prefix even though `concept_id` is left unconstrained. Registered as `GET /apollo/teacher/classroom/{search_space_id}/heatmap` / `.../struggles` in `apollo/api.py` (see the `apollo/` root row), gated by `require_course_teacher`. |
| `apollo/hoot_bridge/` | `session_init.py` | Hoot→Apollo handoff: resolve the course's candidate concepts from `apollo_concepts WHERE …search_space_id` → `infer_concept_id` → DB problem selection → session (with `apollo_sessions.concept_id` populated) + attempt rows. **WU-6A3:** the session-start problem selection now routes through `overseer.select_problem_personalized` (flag-gated, byte-identical when OFF) instead of `select_problem`, so the personalization wedge fires at session start. |
| `apollo/subjects/` | `__init__.py`, `curriculum_db.py`, `fluid_mechanics/concepts/bernoulli_principle/`, `macroeconomics/`, `calculus_2/` (2026-07-08: 10 concepts / 60 problems, authored from the verified corpus in `apollo/provisioning/corpora/calc2/` under the reversed-provisioning model — premade concept list, reference graphs derived from SymPy-verified worked solutions) | Filesystem concept registry: `canonical_symbols.json`, `normalization_map.json`, `parser_prompt_template.md`, `solver_hints.json`, `forbidden_named_laws.json`, `concept_dag.json`, `misconceptions.json`, `problems/problem_*.json`. `misconceptions.json` (WU-3B authoring source) lists the bernoulli `misc.*` Layer-1 entities, each with an `opposes` target key (e.g. `misc.density_ignored` opposes `cond.incompressibility`) and trigger phrases that double as resolution aliases. The `problem_*.json` reference solutions now carry the WU-3B annotation: an `entity_key` per reference-solution step + a top-level `declared_paths` (one complete ordered path) + `layer1_seeded` marker — additive keys only, written by the WU-3B seeder so the §6.1 validation contract passes and a fresh registry re-import carries the links. **As of WU-4A1, `problem_01.json` also carries an additive top-level `symbolic_mappings` key (`{"d": "2*r"}`)** — the per-problem declared variable-substitution table read by `graph_compare.build_problem_candidates` and passed into `resolve_attempt`'s symbolic tier (the §6.9 `A = pi*r**2` → `eq.circular_area` equivalence resolves only with this mapping; the resolver applies NO global `d=2r` default). The key round-trips through BOTH seeders with ZERO seeder code change (the registry seeder reads the JSON verbatim into `apollo_concept_problems.payload`; the learner-model seeder's `annotate_reference_solution` shallow-copies the payload, preserving it) — pinned by `tests/database/test_graph_compare_symbolic_mappings_roundtrip.py` (real-PG, local Docker only). `load_concept(subject_id, concept_id) -> ConceptDefinition` is the AUTHORING-format reader (kept). As of WU-3D (§8A cutover) the runtime reads concepts/problems from the DB — `curriculum_db.list_course_concepts(db, search_space_id)` / `curriculum_db.load_concept_definition(db, concept_id)` + `problem_selector.list_problems_for_concept`/`select_problem` — so the filesystem layout is now the AUTHORING source ONLY, converted to `apollo_subjects`/`apollo_concepts`/`apollo_concept_problems` rows (migration 018) by `scripts/seed_apollo_concept_registry.py`. `curriculum_db` builds a `ConceptDefinition` from the `apollo_concepts` JSONB/TEXT columns (its `problems_dir` is a sentinel non-existent path — the runtime never globs it) and raises the internal `ConceptNotFoundError` if the row is absent. |
| `apollo/clarification/` | `embedding.py`, `detector.py`, `probe.py`, `pacing.py`, `candidate_assembly.py`, `rescorer.py`, `store.py`, `turn.py`, `leak_guard.py`, `resolve_turn.py` | G2 clarification loop (spec §6.3–§6.6). **`candidate_assembly.py` is the single shared recipe** used by BOTH the chat path and the grading (Done) path: `load_problem_candidates_with_soundness` runs load-bank→dict→specs→build_problem_candidates once and returns `(ProblemInputs, bank_applicable)`; the chat-path entry `load_problem_candidates` is a thin delegate (drops soundness). **Misconception key-prefix invariant (lane B4/Q1, 2026-07-03):** `_misconceptions_dict` re-prefixes each bank row's DB `code` to the canonical `misc.<code>` key form (`{"key": f"misc.{e.code}"}`) because the seeder (`misconception_bank_seed.misconception_entry_to_bank_spec`) STRIPS the `misc.` prefix into the `apollo_misconceptions.code` column (`key.removeprefix("misc.")`, e.g. `density_ignored`). The canonical misconception key everywhere downstream of assembly is `misc.*` — `candidates_from_misconceptions` uses it as the candidate's `canonical_key`, `soundness.is_misconception_key` keys contradiction detection on the `misc.` prefix, the `:Canon` `canon_key` projection is keyed on the prefixed `apollo_kg_entities.canonical_key`, and `misconceptions.json` authors `misc.*` directly. Emitting the bare `code` here left every misconception candidate's `canonical_key` failing `is_misconception_key` → a resolved-to-misconception student node routed to `unsupported_extra` instead of `contradiction_finding` → `build_misconceptions` returned `[]` and no misconception was EVER detectable course-wide (the vacuous-S5 defect on BOTH the grading `done_grading.run_graph_simulation` and clarification `chat` seams, since both consume this one recipe). The bank code is always stripped (never `misc.`-prefixed), so a plain `f"misc.{code}"` cannot double-prefix. `detector.py` computes cosine similarity between residual-node embeddings and candidate embeddings; a node ambiguously close to a candidate (cosine ≥ T_AMBIG 0.50 threshold) is flagged as a `FlaggedNode`. `turn.py` adds an early-exit: if `find_residual_nodes` returns `[]` (all nodes resolve) the function returns immediately without any embedding call. `pacing.py` gates how many probes to surface per turn. `probe.py` composes an answer-blind follow-up question via `draft_reply` and weaves it into the Apollo reply via `clarification_hints`. `rescorer.py` re-scores the student's committed answer on the next turn (`confirmed`/`refuted`/`vague`, capped at clarification method 0.90). `store.py` persists probes + outcomes to the `apollo_clarifications` table (`UNIQUE(attempt_id, node_id)` — one probe per idea; state machine `asked_waiting → {confirmed|refuted|vague}`). `resolve_turn.py` exposes `load_confirmed_resolutions(db, attempt_id)` → `dict[node_id, candidate_key]`, which `run_graph_simulation` threads into `resolve_attempt(confirmed_resolutions=...)` so confirmed nodes clear the abstention floor before fuzzy/LLM tiers fire. `leak_guard.py` is a soft-fail-open leakage backstop that screens clarification replies only (non-raising; the structural answer-blind guarantee in `probe.py` is the primary line). Note: embeddings flag candidates for probing but NEVER grant credit — credit is PROVEN (deterministic tiers) or STUDENT-CONFIRMED via the clarification method only. |
| `*/tests/` | per-subpackage `tests/` dirs + `apollo/tests/` e2e smokes | Most are **skip-marked**: "Tracked in claude_v3_checklist.md item 1; will be re-enabled in test-rewrite phase" (they predate the V3 KGGraph + Neo4j rewrite). |

WU-AAS pairing persistence (migration 032) adds `AuthoredSet` in
`apollo/persistence/models.py`, mapped to `apollo_authored_sets`. It records one
course-scoped problem/solution document pair per `search_space_id,set_index`, with
`status` (`pending|indexing|provisioning|done|failed`) and bounded
`result_summary` JSON for per-problem provisioning outcomes. The ORM mirrors the
repo convention: `_JSONType`, portable BigInteger primary key, FK to
`aita_search_spaces`, and no ORM CHECK constraint duplication.

WU-AAS authored-set label matching starts in
`apollo/provisioning/authored_sets/label_match.py`. It normalizes printed labels
such as `Problem 3`, `Q3`, `3.`, and `Exercise 4(a)` to canonical keys, extracts
problem labels from `CandidateQuestion.label` with a problem-text fallback, and
indexes paired solution chunks by deterministic label matches. A sub-label (the
`a` in `4a`/`4(a)`) attaches ONLY when adjacent to the number — a bare letter
must immediately follow the digit and only the parenthesized form may be
whitespace-separated, so a solution heading like `Solution 1\nM = …` keys as `1`
rather than absorbing the following variable into a spurious `1m`. Ambiguous
labels (zero or multiple distinct chunks) deliberately return no match so the
paired retrieval layer can fall through to doc-scoped retrieval.

## Public interfaces

Provisioning retrieval adapter note: `make_course_retrieve_fn` skips hybrid-search
rows whose `content` is missing or blank before building `GroundingSpan` values.
Those malformed rows are treated as per-span no-ops; they must not raise a
`KeyError` that aborts the whole document.

Mounted in `server.py`: `app.include_router(apollo_router)` + `register_exception_handlers(app)`
(server.py:54, 645-646).

HTTP routes (all defined in `apollo/api.py`):

| Route | Handler | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| `POST /apollo/sessions/from_hoot` | `hoot_bridge.session_init.init_session_from_hoot` | Body `{search_space_id, hoot_transcript, difficulty="intro"}`. Identity from bearer token; membership checked via `require_course_member`. Ends any prior active session. 409 on `NoMatchingConceptError`/`PoolExhaustedError`. |
| `POST /apollo/sessions` | `hoot_bridge.session_init.init_session_direct` | Standalone entry (no Hoot transcript). Body `{search_space_id, concept_id, difficulty, problem_id?}` — `difficulty` (`intro\|standard\|hard`) is REQUIRED (the student always picks). Validates `concept_id` against the course's teachable set (`list_course_concepts`) → 409 `NoMatchingConceptError` if not teachable. With `problem_id`: validates it against the concept's teachable pool (`list_problems_for_concept`: tier-2, non-quarantined) → 404 `problem_not_found` (`ProblemNotFoundError`) on a bad/tier-1/quarantined/foreign id; the attempt records the REQUESTED `difficulty` while the problem keeps its own (same as `handle_next`). Without `problem_id`: `select_problem_personalized` picks from the pool. Shares the row-creation core (`_create_session_with_problem`) with `from_hoot` — ends any prior active session, creates TEACHING session + first `ProblemAttempt`, returns `{session_id, attempt_id, problem}` (byte-compatible with `from_hoot`). Membership-gated (`require_course_member`). |
| `GET /apollo/sessions/{id}` | `handlers.lifecycle.handle_get_session` | Session + problem + full KG + messages. Owner-gated (`require_session_owner`). Neo4j-degraded: KG read failure degrades `kg` to `{"nodes": [], "edges": []}`, rest of the payload unaffected. |
| `POST /apollo/sessions/{id}/chat` | `handlers.chat.handle_chat` | Body `{message}`. Returns `{apollo_reply, kg_entries_added, kg}` (+ optional `intent_pending` / `intent_executed`). Owner-gated (`require_session_owner`). Neo4j-degraded: KG reads degrade to an empty graph/summary, writes are skipped (`kg_entries_added=0`) — the conversational reply always proceeds, never a 500. |
| `POST /apollo/sessions/{id}/done` | `handlers.done.handle_done` | Freeze → grade → XP, then (WU-3C1) stamp `graded_at` on the frozen subgraph as the final, idempotent, post-commit retention write. 422 `review_required` if Done-gate fires. **(WU-4C1)** when `APOLLO_GRAPH_SIM_SHADOW_ENABLED` is on, the shadow graph-simulation chain runs AFTER retention and persists a comparison run + findings ALONGSIDE the unchanged student grade; on a shadow failure it surfaces one of the five new error responses — 503 `resolution_unavailable`/`transcript_audit_unavailable`, 500 `resolution_invalid_output`, 422 `student_graph_invalid`, 409 `reference_graph_invalid` — WITHOUT voiding the already-committed grade (the 503s set `learner_update_pending` for an idempotent retry; the 422/409 do not). **(WU-4C2)** while SHADOW is on the chain ALSO computes the graph-sim candidate rubric (`build_graph_sim_rubric`) + the §6.7 calibration metrics (letter agreement + per-axis/overall deltas, LOGGED as `graph_sim_calibration`, NO new column) + the §6.8 constrained diagnostic, all carried on `ShadowGradeResult`; the DORMANT `APOLLO_GRAPH_SIM_LIVE_ENABLED` (default OFF EVERYWHERE) gates only PROMOTION of the graph-sim `rubric`/`diagnostic_narrative` to student-facing — the build-state response is byte-identical to WU-4C1 (coverage/progress/XP always OLD-path). **Neo4j-degraded (2026-07-11):** the pre-freeze read degrades to an empty graph + skips the Done-gate (fail-open); if degraded AND the transcript grader is off/failed, 503 `coverage_grading_failed` (`stage="kg_unavailable_fallback"`) instead of a fabricated empty-graph grade; the shadow chain is skipped (marker `graph_failure="shadow_failure: neo4j_unavailable"`); `stamp_graded_at` failures (incl. degraded) log-and-continue UNCONDITIONALLY rather than 500 an already-committed grade. Owner-gated (`require_session_owner`). |
| `POST /apollo/sessions/{id}/retry` | `handlers.lifecycle.handle_retry` | Unfreeze, back to TEACHING. Owner-gated (`require_session_owner`). |
| `POST /apollo/sessions/{id}/next` | `handlers.next.handle_next` | New problem at chosen difficulty; advance (REPORT) or abandon (TEACHING/PROBLEM_REVEAL); blocked during SOLVING. Owner-gated (`require_session_owner`). |
| `POST /apollo/sessions/{id}/restart_problem` | `handlers.restart_problem` | Wipes attempt KG (Neo4j `DETACH DELETE`) + messages, same problem. Owner-gated (`require_session_owner`). Neo4j-degraded: NO silent skip — raises `KGUnavailableError` (503 `kg_unavailable`) instead, since the wipe targets the SAME `attempt_id` and a skipped delete would resurface stale KG nodes once Neo4j returns; the Postgres message delete never runs on a degraded wipe (ordering guarantee — nothing half-wiped). |
| `POST /apollo/sessions/{id}/end` | `handlers.lifecycle.handle_end` | Marks ended; per-attempt Neo4j subgraphs PERSIST (§7 retention, WU-3C1) — `restart_problem` is the only explicit wipe; a future janitor prunes old subgraphs. Owner-gated (`require_session_owner`). Its `neo` param is unused — unaffected by Neo4j degraded mode. |
| `GET /apollo/progress` | `handlers.progress` | XP, level, title, next tier threshold. Token-derived identity (`require_user`). **Optional `?search_space_id=N`**: without it the payload is byte-identical to the base era (Hoot callers unaffected, `handle_get_progress`); with it, `require_course_member` is enforced and `handle_get_progress_detail` appends a `detail` block — `mastery` (per-concept `{concept_id, display_name, mastery_avg, entity_count}`, `LearnerState.mastery` averaged over `apollo_learner_state` grouped by `apollo_kg_entities.concept_id`, ordered by concept display_name) and `recent_attempts` (the 10 most recent `result="graded"` `ProblemAttempt` rows for this user+course, newest-first, `{attempt_id, problem_id, concept_id, concept_display_name, difficulty, score, letter, created_at}` — `score`/`letter` read from `diagnostic_report.rubric.overall`, always written on grade regardless of `APOLLO_GRADING_ARTIFACT_ENABLED`). |
| `GET /apollo/concepts?search_space_id=` | `subjects.curriculum_db.list_course_concepts` | Student browse surface — the course's TEACHABLE concepts (`{concepts: [{concept_id, slug, display_name}]}`), each with ≥1 tier-2 non-quarantined problem (the same selectable-pool predicate session entry uses). Membership-gated (`require_course_member`, auto-enroll like `from_hoot`). |
| `GET /apollo/problems?search_space_id=&concept_id=[&difficulty=intro\|standard\|hard]` | `handlers.browse.handle_list_problems` | Student browse surface — one concept's TEACHABLE problem pool (`list_problems_for_concept`: tier-2, non-quarantined), optionally difficulty-filtered, each flagged `attempted` by the caller's own `ProblemAttempt` rows in this course. **Student-safety invariant:** each item carries ONLY `{id, difficulty, problem_text, attempted}` — never `reference_solution` / `given_values` / `target_unknown`. A `concept_id` outside the course's candidate set (`list_course_concepts`) raises `NoMatchingConceptError` (409) rather than leaking cross-course problems. Membership-gated (`require_course_member`). |
| `POST /apollo/sessions/{id}/kg/{entry_id}/challenge` / `paraphrase` / `skip`, `GET .../trace` | `handlers.negotiate` | Negotiable-OLM moves (P3). 404 `kg_entry_not_found` on stale entry ids. Owner-gated (`require_session_owner`). Neo4j-degraded: the three moves (KG-native) raise `KGUnavailableError` (503 `kg_unavailable`, "your session is unaffected; try again shortly") on a degraded store call or snapshot re-read; `GET .../trace` is Postgres-only and unaffected. |
| `GET /apollo/teacher/concepts?search_space_id=`, `POST /apollo/teacher/concepts`, `PATCH /apollo/teacher/concepts/{concept_id}`, `DELETE /apollo/teacher/concepts/{concept_id}` | `provisioning.concepts_api` | WU-TCA teacher concept authoring, gated by `require_course_teacher`. A teacher writes the course's concept list (display_name + migration-038 `description`) ahead of content: create mints an underscore slug (`mint_slug`), 409s on a `norm_slug`-duplicate within the course, and reuses `tag_mint_persist.resolve_or_create_concept` (auto-creates the course's first `Subject`); list returns every non-provisional concept with `problem_count`/`has_teachable_problems` (authored-but-empty concepts are matcher targets via `list_registered_concepts` but invisible to students until a tier-2 problem attaches); update edits name/description only — the slug is stable across renames; delete 409s when ANY `ConceptProblem`s or `KGEntity`s exist (provisioned-content teardown belongs to the authored-set delete flow). The reserved `provisional.inventory` row is invisible here (404/list-excluded). Tests: `apollo/provisioning/tests/test_concepts_api.py`. |
| `POST /apollo/authored-sets`, `GET /apollo/authored-sets`, `GET /apollo/authored-sets/{set_id}`, `POST /apollo/authored-sets/{set_id}/problems/{problem_id}/approve`, `DELETE /apollo/authored-sets/{set_id}` | `provisioning.authored_sets.api` | WU-AAS paired problem/solution set surface, gated by `require_course_teacher` (role='teacher'; no auto-enroll fallback) — a plain course member can no longer call these. Create accepts multipart `problem` PDF (required) + `solution` PDF (optional, `File(None)` — PR B: the intended teacher flow is problem-only, letting the pipeline auto-generate held-for-review reference solutions) and `search_space_id`, writes an `AuthoredSet`, indexes the problem doc (and the solution doc when provided) hidden, then schedules in-process background provisioning. Poll endpoints return status + bounded `result_summary`; the per-set GET enriches each live problem entry with capped `problem_text` + the whitelisted `authored_review` projection (`review`: current `required`, `reason`, `approved_reference`, `augmented`, and trimmed drafts while held) for the teacher review UI. Approve promotes a held Tier-1 problem using the teacher-selected OCR or generated reference. Delete is terminal-status only (`done`/`failed`) — 409 while `pending`/`indexing`/`provisioning` (the in-flight background task writes Neo4j `:Canon` nodes outside the PG transaction, so a mid-run delete would orphan them); on success it removes the `AuthoredSet`, the `ConceptProblem`s it minted (ids read from `result_summary["problems"]`), and the two hidden reference docs (chunks cascade); the shared per-concept `:Canon` projection is deliberately left intact. |

Key service entry points:
- `parse_utterance(utterance, *, concept: ConceptDefinition, attempt_id: int, graph_context: GraphContext | None = None, model=None) -> tuple[list[Node], list[Edge]]` — one strict-json_schema GPT-4o call → typed nodes + all four typed edges (provenance-tagged); `graph_context` (optional) supplies prior-attempt nodes for cross-turn edge linking — `chat.py` builds and threads it on every turn (WU-2B). Raises `ParserCouldNotExtractError` only when a *non-trivial* utterance yields zero entries.
- `build_graph_context(graph: KGGraph) -> GraphContext` (pure, `apollo/parser/graph_context.py`) — projects a read subgraph into the parser's prior-attempt context, deriving a short per-type label and skipping any id that would collide with the `^n\d+$` ordinal namespace (`is_safe_context_id`).
- `KGStore.write_nodes(*, attempt_id, nodes, source, user_id=None, search_space_id=None) -> int` (count CREATED; cross-turn-reused ids excluded; WU-3C1 scoping kwargs are keyword-only + default `None` = back-compat, injected as Layer-2 node props plus an always-present `created_at`) / `write_edges(*, attempt_id, edges, source) -> WriteEdgesResult` (`written`/`dropped`/`invalid`/`reasons`; `int()`-coercible to `written` for back-compat; validates before CREATE, logs every rejection) / `read_graph(*, attempt_id) -> KGGraph` / `delete_subgraph(*, attempt_id)` / `stamp_graded_at(*, attempt_id) -> int` (WU-3C1; sets `graded_at` on the frozen subgraph, idempotent, raises `RetentionError` on Neo4j failure) / `summarize_for_apollo(*, attempt_id) -> str` / `freeze(session_id)` / `unfreeze(session_id)` / `mark_node_disputed` / `paraphrase_node` / `skip_node` / `get_node_trace`.
- `apollo.knowledge_graph.canon_projection.project_canon(db, neo, *, search_space_id=None, concept_id=None) -> CanonProjectionResult` (WU-3C1; idempotent `:Canon` MERGE from Postgres entities; raises `CanonProjectionError`; refuses an unscoped seed via `ValueError`) — pure helpers `entity_to_canon_spec`/`canon_spec_to_row`, async `load_entity_specs`/`merge_specs`. CLI: `scripts/seed_canon_projection.py`.
- `apollo.resolution.resolve_attempt(student_graph, candidates, *, confirmed_resolutions=None, fuzzy_threshold=0.9, symbolic_mappings=None, nli_ctx=None) -> ResolutionResult` (WU-3C2; the §5 resolver — pure + deterministic; per-node `ResolvedNode{node_id, resolution, resolved_key, resolved_canon_key, method, confidence}`; `ResolutionResult.resolved_edges()` yields the resolved-with-`:Canon`-key subset; `result.llm_calls == 0` always (Task 4, 2026-06-29 retired the silent one-LLM-adjudication path — `adjudication.py` deleted; a post-tier, non-clarified node stays `unresolved`; the clarification loop occupies that band); never raises for a non-match. `confirmed_resolutions: dict[str,str] | None = None` maps `node_id → candidate_key` for nodes whose mapping was authorised by a live clarification exchange (Task 3 / §5.3); applied BEFORE the content tiers; a type-incompatible or unknown key is silently ignored. `symbolic_mappings` is PER-PROBLEM declared data — `None` → `{}` (no global default; the §6.9 `d=2r` case resolves only when the caller passes it). Candidate builders `build_candidate_set`/`candidates_from_reference_solution`/`candidates_from_misconceptions`; `METHOD_CONFIDENCE_CAP`. **Phase 1a (derived equation-alignment tier, 2026-06-23):** a new deterministic `derived` resolution tier (`apollo/resolution/equation_alignment.py::match_equation_alignment`) sits in `_content_match` BETWEEN the sign-exact symbolic tier and the lexical alias/fuzzy tiers. For an equation node it solves each reference equation's zero-form for each free symbol (`solve(Eq(r,0), x)`, str-sorted branches) and tests whether any solved branch reproduces the student's zero-form — under the DECLARED `symbolic_mappings` ONLY (no numeric-given substitution; floats Rational-ized; every SymPy call `try/except → non-match`, mirroring `tiers._symbolic_equiv`). So a student equation stated as a *solved/rearranged* form of a reference equation (e.g. `realGDP = nomGDP/(PI/100)` for `deflator = (nomGDP/realGDP)*100`) resolves to the governing entity instead of landing `unresolved` (which previously dropped every incident edge). Placement AFTER the symbolic tier is load-bearing: substitution-collapsible forms still report `symbolic@0.98`; only genuine solve-for-variable forms report the new method. `RESOLUTION_METHODS` and `METHOD_CONFIDENCE_CAP` gain `"derived"` (cap **0.95**, between `symbolic`@0.98 and `alias`@0.92); `_resolved` re-derives confidence from the cap dynamically. Shadow-gated (`APOLLO_GRAPH_SIM_SHADOW_ENABLED`); no student-facing grade change. The no-infra before/after metrics harness `scripts/econ_grading_delta.py` (D4) drives the real macroeconomics Q4 `nominal_vs_real_gdp/problem_01` through `build_problem_candidates → resolve_attempt → build_student_canonical → grade_attempt` and records the BEFORE/AFTER delta (rearranged deflator: `unresolved`→`derived`, `dropped_edge_count` 1→0, `edge_coverage` 0→0.25, `usage` 0→1.0). **`find_residual_nodes` (Task 6, 2026-06-30):** `apollo.resolution.find_residual_nodes(nodes, candidates, *, fuzzy_threshold=0.9, symbolic_mappings=None, nli_ctx=None) -> list[Node]` is a public helper exported from `apollo.resolution` that exposes the deterministic-tier residual filter: it runs `_content_match` per node and returns the nodes no tier matched. This is the clarification detector's input (Task 6 / `apollo/clarification/detector.py`); by reusing `_content_match` directly, the ambiguous-node banding stays in exact lockstep with grading-time resolution.
- `apollo.provisioning.resolve_candidate(db, *, search_space_id, concept_id, candidate, embed_fn, judge_fn, ingest_run_id=None, exclude_entity_ids=None) -> DedupVerdict{verdict, method, similarity, matched_entity_id}` (WU-3B2c; the §8B.5 course-local dedup ladder — slug-exact → `scope_summary` cosine → injected LLM-judge band tiebreaker). **Pool scoping is the load-bearing invariant (PR2 — the 2026-06-30 false-merge fix):** `_in_course_entities` applies `Subject.search_space_id` AND `KGEntity.concept_id == :concept_id` in SQL BEFORE any cosine, so two COURSES never merge (the `test_cross_course_*` property) AND two CONCEPTS of one course never merge (no foreign-set binding / cross-concept fusion). `exclude_entity_ids` additionally drops entities minted earlier in the SAME mint, so two distinct nodes of one problem (the `m≡M` fusion) can't fuse — only PRE-EXISTING entities are dedup targets. Ties break to the lowest `KGEntity.id` (first-writer-wins); writes exactly ONE `apollo_dedup_decisions` row per call (`similarity` NULL for the slug tier / the empty-inventory distinct). `embed_fn`/`judge_fn` are SYNC injected stubs (`embed_text` / a `cheap_chat` adapter) — Tier-1 tests make NO network call. Reads + audits ONLY (no scrape/mint/upsert — 3B2d; no run-counter increment — 3B2g). Constants `EMBED_MERGE_THRESHOLD=0.92` / `EMBED_JUDGE_BAND=(0.82,0.92)` in `apollo.provisioning.dedup_constants`.
- `apollo.provisioning.scrape_questions(chunks, *, chat_fn) -> ScrapeResult{candidates, scraped_count, parse_failures}` + `apollo.provisioning.write_tier1_problems(db, candidates, *, concept_id, search_space_id) -> int` (WU-3B2d stage 1; the LLM scrape → Tier-1 `apollo_concept_problems` inventory). `scrape_questions` runs one injected `chat_fn` pass per `AITAChunk` (READ ONLY — NEVER re-indexes) into `CandidateQuestion`s, fail-SOFT per chunk (malformed JSON / invalid candidate → `parse_failures`, never a half-parsed row). `CandidateQuestion.label` is an optional printed problem number/label captured from the LLM record for authored-set label matching; omitted legacy scrape records still validate with `label=None`. `write_tier1_problems` writes `tier=1` EXPLICIT (the safety trap — the ORM default is 2/teachable; `list_problems_for_concept` excludes Tier-1), course-scoped by the denormalized `search_space_id`, **idempotent** on a content-derived `problem_code = f"scrape.{chunk_content_hash}"` (`sha256` of the normalized chunk content — survives a re-index; a re-run inserts ZERO rows via SELECT-then-skip). The NOT-NULL `concept_id` is a per-course reserved `provisional.inventory` concept (`resolve_or_create_provisional_concept`), never teachable. `chat_fn` is injected (mocked in Tier-1 — NO network). The Stage-1 scrape system prompt (`orchestrator._SCRAPE_SYSTEM_PROMPT`) is now SCHEMA-EXPLICIT — it declares the 6 LLM-supplied `CandidateQuestion` keys (`problem_text`/`given_values`/`target_unknown`/`difficulty`/`concept_slug`/`label`), a JSON array with NO markdown fences (the prior vague one-liner produced 0 candidates against a real model) — AND SUBJECT-AGNOSTIC (2026-07-09): its core task is "extract EVERY question a student could be asked to answer" with study-guide review bullets / define-explain-compare prompts / true-false items enumerated as first-class, because the prior "practice problem"/"solvable problems" framing made models at ANY tier (gpt-4o-mini AND gpt-4o, temp 0) return a literal `[]` on a qualitative MGMT study guide (prod ingest run 1 scraped 0 of ~38 extractable questions; the framing reframe recovered 38/38 while an appended exception clause recovered only 3 — fix the primary framing, don't bolt on exceptions). A qualitative question carries `given_values={}` and a phrase-valued `target_unknown`; `_TRIAGE_SYSTEM_PROMPT` is de-biased the same way ("questions ... quantitative exercises OR qualitative review/discussion", not "solvable quantitative practice problems"). `test_scrape_prompt_declares_candidate_question_fields` pins the field contract.
- `apollo.provisioning.authored_sets.indexing.index_authored_doc(db, *, search_space_id, file_bytes, title, set_index, role) -> int` (WU-AAS Task 5) indexes one paired authored problem/solution PDF into `aita_documents`/`aita_chunks` while deliberately bypassing the teacher weekly wrapper. It runs `TeacherPDFIngestor` with `ocr.get_ocr_provider_from_env()` (so `OCR_PROVIDER=openai` selects OpenAI vision), then `AITAIndexingService.prepare_for_indexing` → checkpointed `embed_and_persist_chunks` → `finalize_document`, and finally overrides the document status to `{"state": "apollo_reference"}`. The deterministic `unique_id = authored-set:{search_space_id}:{set_index}:{role}` reuses the same document row for a re-upload; no `TeacherUpload`, supersede, week activation, or generic provisioning enqueue is created.
- `apollo.provisioning.tag_and_mint(db, pair, *, chat_fn, embed_fn) -> MintPlan{concept_id, concept_slug, authored_symbols, minted_entity_ids, merged_entity_keys, prereq_pairs, misconception_keys, dropped_prereq_pairs}` (WU-3B2d stage 4; tag/mint over an ALREADY-approved `ApprovedPair{problem, search_space_id, solution_source, misconceptions}` — 3B2e produces a compatible value later, tested here with a fixture). LLM-drafts the concept tag (slug→BIGINT, all persistence keyed on the BIGINT per §6) + prereq edges, AUTHORS `apollo_concepts.canonical_symbols`/`normalization_map` first-writer-wins UNION (gate-4 non-vacuity), mints reference + `kind='misconception'` entities by REUSING two frozen seed converters (`reference_solution_to_entities`/`misconceptions_to_entities`; prereqs are LLM-drafted, not via `concept_dag_to_prereqs`), dedups EACH candidate via `resolve_candidate` BEFORE upsert (a `merged` verdict reuses the existing id), passing the ids resolved EARLIER in this mint as `exclude_entity_ids` so two distinct nodes of one problem never fuse against each other (PR2 Part B). §1.4 course-scoped (every write `search_space_id`/`concept_id`-scoped). Misconception-storage DEVIATION (ADJ #2): `kind='misconception'` `apollo_kg_entities` rows, NOT `apollo_misconceptions`. Stage 4 normalizes the LLM tag draft's BARE reference-node ids (e.g. `bernoulli`) to their prefixed canonical keys (`eq.bernoulli`) via `_bare_id_aliases` (reusing the frozen `_entity_key_for_step`) before `insert_prereqs`/`link_opposes`, because the tag prompt never exposes the prefix scheme. Genuinely-unmappable keys still fail closed as `TagMintError`. `apollo_entity_prereqs` holds TWO kinds of edge, distinguished by endpoint `apollo_kg_entities.kind`: CONCEPT-LEVEL edges (seed path, `concept_dag_to_prereqs` — both endpoints `kind='concept'`, cross-concept curriculum ordering) and REF-NODE-LEVEL edges (auto path, `tag_and_mint` — within-problem step structure). Both are valid; there is intentionally no discriminator column. `read_learner_profile` loads only WITHIN-CONCEPT edges, so it consumes the auto ref-node edges and excludes the seed cross-concept concept-level edges — the two kinds never conflate in `prereqs_mastered`. Guard: `apollo/provisioning/tests/test_prereq_edge_kinds.py`. An explicit `edge_kind` column is a possible Phase-2+ change, not required for this contract. FAIL-CLOSED `TagMintError` on an unmappable LLM tag / `opposes_entity_key` (no silent mislink; the caller owns the txn); a prereq edge naming an unminted key is dropped, not fatal (2026-06-30). ACYCLICITY GUARD (`_acyclic_prereq_pairs`, before `insert_prereqs`): a resolvable prereq edge that would introduce a self-loop or close a directed CYCLE in `apollo_entity_prereqs` is dropped + logged (`tag_mint_dropped_cyclic_prereqs`); the check resolves each endpoint through `key_to_id` so a dedup MERGE that collapses two distinct keys onto one entity id (the `m≡M` fusion) is caught as a self-loop, and `MintPlan.prereq_pairs` reflects the kept acyclic subset. The composite PK `(from_entity_id, to_entity_id)` permits both `(A,B)` and `(B,A)` (and a self-loop) with no DB-level acyclicity, so without this guard a single mint's drafted edges persist as-is. **CROSS-MINT SEEDING (2026-07-01 fix):** `_acyclic_prereq_pairs` is no longer scoped to a single mint's own draft only — `tag_and_mint` now seeds its `adj` from `tag_mint_persist.load_concept_prereq_adjacency(db, concept_id=..., entity_ids=...)`, a read of this concept's already-PERSISTED `apollo_entity_prereqs` rows, BEFORE folding in this mint's own edges. This closes the gap where a SECOND mint into the same shared concept could draft the REVERSE of an EARLIER mint's already-committed edge (mint 1: A→B; mint 2: B→A) and pass its own in-mint-only check — a cross-mint cycle is now caught at mint time. `insert_prereqs` (`tag_mint_persist.py`) adds a second, defense-in-depth guard at the writer boundary: it re-derives the full persisted concept subgraph itself (also via `load_concept_prereq_adjacency`) and re-checks each edge before insert, dropping (and logging as the distinct event `tag_mint_dropped_persisted_cycle_prereqs`) any edge that would close a cycle against everything already committed for the concept — the writer does not trust its caller either. `insert_prereqs`'s returned `dropped` list now includes both the pre-existing cross-concept-scope drops and this persisted-cycle category. ENDPOINT CONCEPT-SCOPE GUARD (PR2b — the 2026-06-30 foreign-binding fix, #74; `partition_prereqs_by_concept_scope`, run BEFORE the acyclicity guard and re-checked at the writer boundary inside `insert_prereqs`): every prereq edge endpoint must resolve to an entity OWNED BY this `concept_id`. A dedup `merged` verdict can point `key_to_id` at a FOREIGN-concept entity id — that key is still 'resolvable', so the unminted-key drop never catches it and the edge would persist pointing into another concept's subgraph (dead weight the reader filters at `personalization_read.py:146-153`; and, since `:Canon` is a NODE-ONLY projection, the foreign target entity is absent from this concept's `:Canon` nodes, so a student's correct step has no reference node to match). The writer therefore enforces concept scope exactly as the reader does (both reduce to `KGEntity.concept_id == concept_id` on BOTH endpoints): a cross-concept edge is DROPPED (WARNING `tag_mint_dropped_cross_concept_prereqs`) and excluded from `MintPlan.prereq_pairs`. ORDER MATTERS: the cross-concept drop runs BEFORE `_acyclic_prereq_pairs`, so a foreign endpoint can never sit in the acyclicity reachability graph as a phantom BRIDGE across two cross-concept edges and fake a cycle that discards a legitimate within-concept edge. With PR2's concept-scoped dedup pool this defense-in-depth guard should never fire; if it does, an upstream scoping invariant regressed. ALL THREE drop reasons — unresolvable-key, cross-concept-endpoint, and cyclic (acyclicity guard) — are now SURFACED on `MintPlan.dropped_prereq_pairs` (previously INFO/WARNING-logged only), so the 3B2g handoff sees exactly which drafted edges were refused. NO promotion (3B2g runs the lint over the `MintPlan`). `chat_fn`/`embed_fn` injected (mocked in Tier-1 — NO network). The stage-1/stage-4 public surface (`scrape_questions`/`write_tier1_problems`/`CandidateQuestion`/`ScrapeResult`, `tag_and_mint`/`ApprovedPair`/`MintPlan`/`TagMintError`) is RE-EXPORTED at the package level from `apollo/provisioning/__init__.py`, so the `apollo.provisioning.<name>` paths above resolve directly (mirroring the existing `resolve_candidate`/`run_promotion_lint` re-exports). The orchestrator's `_tag_mint_chat_fn` now sends a SCHEMA-EXPLICIT `_TAG_MINT_SYSTEM_PROMPT` (declaring `concept_slug` REQUIRED + `display_name`/`prereqs`) plus a `response_format` json_schema (`build_tag_schema`, strict) — previously it sent NO system prompt and NO schema, so a real model emitted no `concept_slug` → `TagMintError`; `test_tag_mint_chat_fn_sends_system_prompt_and_schema` pins the wiring.
- **Auto-provisioning Phase 2 — STRUCTURE-AWARE stage-1 scrape:** stage 1 no longer scrapes one LLM call per retrieval micro-chunk. The orchestrator loads chunk section metadata (`section_path`, `chunk_type` alongside `id`/`content`/`document_id`/`page_number`) and `apollo.provisioning.scrape_document(chunk_rows, *, chat_fn, triage_chat_fn, max_sections, min_candidates, structured=True, section_char_cap=APOLLO_SCRAPE_SECTION_CHAR_CAP) -> ScrapeResult` (a) reconstructs the document's real sections via `section_grouping.group_into_sections` (a `chunk_type='heading'` chunk OR a non-empty `section_path` change opens a section; no-heading/no-path degrades to one whole-doc section; heading text is the title, excluded from body), (b) splits every section over `APOLLO_SCRAPE_SECTION_CHAR_CAP` (default 2500 chars) into page-boundary windows before triage, falling back to character windows with ~200-character overlap when page metadata is absent or one page exceeds the cap, (c) triages the resulting section/window list ONCE (`section_triage.triage_sections`, FAIL-OPEN — a malformed/empty triage response marks every section problem-likely at equal priority, never aborts) to rank + concept-label sections, then (d) scrapes whole sections/windows (`scrape_section`) — problem-likely first (sort `(not is_problem_likely, -priority, index)`), widening into NOT-likely sections only while candidates < `APOLLO_SCRAPE_MIN_CANDIDATES` (default 3), capped at `APOLLO_SCRAPE_MAX_SECTIONS` (default 120) calls/doc. Overlap can surface the same question twice; the existing downstream content `problem_hash` gate merges it. Same fail-soft contract as the per-chunk path (bad JSON / non-array / invalid record → `parse_failures`). This replaces the per-micro-chunk scrape (~92% of spend was the ~200-tok prompt re-sent per ~17-char fragment, tripping the 2M `PER_DOCUMENT_TOKEN_CEILING`, and no call ever saw a whole problem) — resolving the Phase-1 "unbounded per-doc scrape fan-out" gap. The per-candidate idempotency key is now `scrape.<section_content_hash>.<ordinal>` (ordinal assigned over a section's candidates sorted by `chunk_content_hash(problem_text)`, so a re-run yields the SAME key↔problem mapping), carried VERBATIM in the existing `CandidateQuestion.chunk_content_hash` field — `write_tier1_problems`/`_problem_code_for`/`_find_tier1_row_id` are unchanged and there is NO migration (subsystem dormant: `APOLLO_AUTOPROVISION_ENABLED` OFF + 0 replicas). The drop-in remains at the shared `scrape_document` seam, so both generic and authored-set orchestrators receive the guard without changing the returned `ScrapeResult(candidates, scraped_count, parse_failures)`; stages 2–5 and the §4b decision logic do NOT change. `_TRIAGE_SYSTEM_PROMPT` is added; `_SCRAPE_SYSTEM_PROMPT` is reframed for whole-section input and declares the 6 LLM-supplied keys, including optional `label`. Triage's `concept_slug` is a HINT only (`scrape_section` falls back LLM-value → triage hint → `provisional.inventory`); stage-4 `tag_and_mint` stays the authoritative concept resolver. Bounds + flag live in `cost_constants` (`APOLLO_SCRAPE_MAX_SECTIONS`/`APOLLO_SCRAPE_MIN_CANDIDATES`/`APOLLO_SCRAPE_SECTION_CHAR_CAP`/`structured_scrape_enabled()`); `APOLLO_STRUCTURED_SCRAPE=0` instantly reverts stage 1 to the legacy per-chunk `scrape_questions`. `scrape_document` is re-exported from `apollo/provisioning/__init__.py`.
- **Auto-provisioning Phase 1 scope / known gaps:** Phase 1 makes the pipeline RUN end-to-end (BLOCKER+H1 key normalization, abort→reject robustness, H4 two-kind prereq contract). DEFERRED: H2 (require `content.symbolic` for equation steps), H3 misconception WIRING (`misconceptions=[]` today; gated by `APOLLO_MISCONCEPTION_ENABLED`, a no-op until chat wiring), the `misconceptions_to_entities` KeyError→named-error hardening (dormant; deferred with H3 to avoid touching the frozen §8 converter), H5 (dedup re-embeds the course pool per candidate), unbounded per-doc scrape fan-out, the scrape-all-chunks vs week-gated-grounding scope asymmetry, the dedup cosine NaN guard, and the LOW hygiene items. Safe to defer: the subsystem is dormant in prod (`APOLLO_AUTOPROVISION_ENABLED` OFF + 0 replicas), so no auto-provisioned data exists to be affected.
- `apollo.provisioning.find_or_generate(db, question, *, retrieve_fn, chat_fn, augment_recall=False) -> ReferenceSolutionDraft{solution_source, reference_solution, grounding, provenance, augmented_problem_text?, augmented_target_unknown?}` (WU-3B2e stage 2; the §8B retrieve-first-then-RAG-generate solution drafter). retrieve-FIRST (a `carries_solution` span → extraction `chat_fn` → `solution_source='extracted'`) then RAG-GENERATE fallback (`chat_fn` over the question + the SAME retrieved spans → `'generated'`, grounding carries those spans for the stage-3 Phase-B judge). The generated `reference_solution` is `Problem.model_validate`-checked before a draft returns; FAIL-CLOSED `SolutionDraftError` on a retrieve-empty + unparseable/empty/Problem-invalid generate (NEVER an empty-step draft). `augment_recall` is default OFF: that path retains the original generation prompt, one-key schema, one call, and no augmentation fields. The authored-set orchestrator alone opts in: `build_solution_schema(augmentation=True)` adds nullable rewritten problem/target fields, the prompt extends recall/definition/statement questions into explain-why questions, and a zero-`procedure_step` first draft receives at most one deterministic retry. Augmentation applies only when a non-empty rewritten problem and at least one reasoning `procedure_step` are both present; otherwise the rewrite is discarded. A missing augmented target falls back to the original question target (never the rewritten full question). The prompt requires disciplinary first-principles reasoning and forbids fabricated course/instructor attribution. Also `apollo.provisioning.solution_hash(draft) -> str` (`sha256` over canonical-JSON `reference_solution` — the `(chunk_content_hash, solution_hash)` idempotency key 3B2g writes on) and `apollo.provisioning.build_approved_pair(question, draft, *, search_space_id) -> tag_mint.ApprovedPair` (assembles the `Problem`-validatable pair, applies accepted augmented text, stamps `solution_source`, IMPORTS the REAL `ApprovedPair`). `retrieve_fn`/`chat_fn` injected (mocked in Tier-1 — NO network, NO DB write). `GroundingSpan{text, document_id?, page?, chunk_content_hash?, carries_solution=False}` is the frozen course-material span value. The Stage-2 extract/generate system prompts DECLARE the `ReferenceStep`/`Problem` output shape (every step's `step`/`entry_type`/`id`/`content`/`depends_on` keys + the per-`entry_type` content fields, sourced from `NODE_CONTENT_TYPES`); `strict=False` because `content` is an open per-type dict and `Problem.model_validate` stays the hard inner enforcer. `_SOLUTION_EXTRACT_SYSTEM_PROMPT` is unchanged by augmentation.
- **Authored problem/solution sets (WU-AAS) — paired-solution retrieval seam:** `apollo/provisioning/authored_sets/paired_retrieval.py` adds `load_solution_chunks(db, solution_document_id=...)`, `chunk_ocr_confidence(db, document_id=...)`, and `make_paired_solution_retrieve_fn(db, solution_document_id, label_index, page_conf, top_k=6)`. `solution_document_id` is `int | None` (PR B1): `None` (no solution PDF uploaded, or a same-content-hash upload the caller discarded — PR B2) short-circuits `load_solution_chunks`/`chunk_ocr_confidence` to empty without a query, and the returned `retrieve(question)` always yields `()` so `find_or_generate` falls through to its generate branch. When a solution doc IS paired, `retrieve` first resolves the scraped/regex problem label through `label_match.match_solution_label`; if exactly one solution chunk matches, it returns `GroundingSpan(carries_solution=True, document_id=<solution doc>, page=<chunk page>, chunk_content_hash=<content hash>)` and records `retrieve.last_match_method="label"` plus `retrieve.last_min_conf`. Otherwise it runs a semantic top-k against `aita_chunks` filtered directly by `AITAChunk.document_id == solution_document_id`, using the shared `_halfvec_cosine_distance` expression and `embed_text`, and marks those spans `carries_solution=False` (PR B3 — an unconfirmed semantic guess is not a confirmed printed solution, so it rides along as generation context instead of taking the extract branch); it intentionally does NOT call `retrieval.document_visibility.active_document_conditions`, because authored solution docs are hidden from student RAG but must remain readable for paired grounding. Empty retrieval returns `()` so `find_or_generate` falls back to `solution_source='generated'`. Tests cover the label branch (`carries_solution=True`), the semantic-fallback branch (`carries_solution=False`), the `solution_document_id=None` branch, the empty branch, and a pgvector-backed distractor-doc case proving document scoping.
- **Authored problem/solution sets (WU-AAS) — OCR-confidence verification seam:** `apollo/provisioning/authored_sets/verification.py` adds `verify_against_generated(db, candidate, draft, min_conf, problem_low_conf, match_method, metered_chat, conf_threshold) -> VerificationVerdict`. High-confidence extracted references return immediately. Low-confidence solution grounding, a low-confidence problem document, **or `min_conf=None`** (a page missing from `page_debug` — no OCR confidence signal at all; treated fail-closed as LOW confidence rather than silently skipped) triggers an independent `find_or_generate` call with an empty retrieve function so the generated comparison does not see the OCR'd solution text. Identical normalized final-answer strings are trusted without an extra judge call; otherwise `metered_chat.cheap` compares the extracted and generated references for material equivalence. Unparseable judge output fails closed to `review_required=True`, `reason="ocr_divergence"`, and carries the generated alternative via `generated_alt` for the Task-8 orchestration hold-for-review path. The seam is compute-only: it writes no DB rows, mutates no KG state, and is mocked in Tier-1 tests.
- **Authored problem/solution sets (WU-AAS) — orchestration seam:** `apollo/provisioning/authored_sets/orchestrator.py` adds `run_authored_set_provisioning(db, neo, *, search_space_id, problem_document_id, solution_document_id, metered_chat, embed_fn=None, conf_threshold=0.6) -> ProvisioningReport`. `solution_document_id: int | None` (PR B1) — `None` means every candidate grounds against no solution spans, so `find_or_generate` always takes its generate branch (`solution_source='generated'`, held for review — the product policy is unchanged: generated solutions ALWAYS need teacher approval, never auto-promoted). It resolves the per-course `provisional.inventory` concept, loads solution chunks into the deterministic label index, scrapes the problem document with the shared structured scrape prompts, writes Tier-1 inventory, then processes each candidate through paired-solution `find_or_generate(augment_recall=True)` → low-OCR `verify_against_generated` → `validate_pair` → `tag_and_mint` → `promote`. **`verify_against_generated` and `validate_pair` both run ONLY when `draft.solution_source == "extracted"`** (2026-07-11 fix) — a `generated` draft has no pair to validate (no grounding spans to entail against), so the pairing gate is skipped entirely and the candidate flows straight to the `review_required` check below with `reason="generated_no_match"`; before this fix `validate_pair` ran unconditionally and its Phase-B faithfulness judge fail-closed (REJECT) on every generated draft's empty grounding, so NO problem-only (no solution doc) candidate could ever reach `held_for_review`. The promoted Tier-2 row records its TRUE provenance: the orchestrator threads `pair.solution_source` into `promote` (so a paired-EXTRACTED reference persists `solution_source='extracted'` instead of the generic `'generated'` default; `promote` writes the threaded value only when the Tier-1 row has none yet, never overwriting an ingest-stamped source — `test_authored_set_orchestrator.test_authored_set_label_extract_promotes` + `test_promote.test_promote_persists_threaded_solution_source` pin it). Trusted extracted references can promote to tier 2; generated references or divergent low-confidence OCR references are held at tier 1 with `ConceptProblem.provenance["authored_review"]` carrying `reason`, `ocr_confidence`, `match_method`, `ocr_draft`, `generated_alt`, and `augmented`. For an augmented hold only, the Tier-1 payload replaces `problem_text`/`target_unknown` with the explain-why versions, preserves the originals as `problem_text_original`/`target_unknown_original`, and stamps `payload.augmented="explain_why"`; unaugmented hold payloads are not copied or modified. Held problems deliberately skip `tag_and_mint` and `promote`, so no canonical KG mutation happens before teacher approval. Per-problem failure/atomicity (2026-07-01 fix): `_process_authored_candidate` (`orchestrator.py`) now runs its `tag_and_mint` call inside a nested SAVEPOINT (`db.begin_nested()`), so a fail-closed `TagMintError` — raised AFTER `tag_and_mint` has already flushed partial concept/`KGEntity`/`apollo_dedup_decisions` rows for that candidate — rolls back only that candidate's writes instead of surviving into the set's end-of-run commit as orphaned KG rows (unreachable by any promoted `ConceptProblem`, yet live dedup targets for the next candidate); a `CanonProjectionError` from the later `promote` call is deliberately OUTSIDE this savepoint and still propagates as a run-level failure. Per-problem results are bounded `ProblemResult` rows (`promoted`/`rejected`/`held_for_review`) with aggregate counts for Task 9 persistence/API status. The helper name resolved from Task 6 is `chunk_ocr_confidence` (not the plan placeholder `page_ocr_confidence`).
- **Authored problem/solution sets (WU-AAS) — HTTP/background/approve seam:** `apollo/provisioning/authored_sets/api.py` exposes the mounted `/apollo/authored-sets` endpoints. `create_authored_set` authenticates with `require_user` + `require_course_teacher` (role='teacher' membership; a plain member 403s), persists `AuthoredSet(status="pending")`, and schedules `_run_set_background`; the background task owns a fresh `get_async_session()`, transitions `pending → indexing → provisioning → done|failed`, calls `index_authored_doc` for the problem doc always and the solution doc only when one was uploaded, then persists `run_authored_set_provisioning(...).model_dump()` in `result_summary`. **Optional solution + same-doc guard (PR B, 2026-07-11):** `solution: UploadFile | None = File(None)` — when absent, solution-role indexing is skipped entirely, `AuthoredSet.solution_document_id` is left NULL, and provisioning is handed `solution_document_id=None`. When a solution file IS provided, its `content_hash` (the same hash `_doc_content_hash` already computes for `IngestRun.content_hash`) is compared against the problem doc's; an exact match (teacher uploaded the same file for both roles) is treated as if no solution were provided — `solution_document_id` stays NULL, a structured `authored_set_same_doc_solution_guard` warning is logged, and `result_summary["same_doc_solution_guard"]` carries a teacher-facing note — instead of grounding questions against their own prose. Every `solution_document_id`/`document_id` consumer in this file (`persist_page_evidence` calls, the GET detail/list rows, the DELETE doc-id collection at `doc_ids = [... if d is not None]`) is NULL-safe. Per-candidate failures are isolated to a single `rejected` `ProblemResult` rather than aborting the whole set: `_process_authored_candidate` catches `SolutionDraftError` (solution draft) and `TagMintError` (the mint draft — e.g. a hallucinated concept tag or an `opposes_entity_key` resolving to no entity; the prereq-key case is dropped inside `tag_and_mint`, not raised); only infra-level `CanonProjectionError` from `promote` propagates to fail the run. `approve_held_problem` first validates the fetched `ConceptProblem` actually belongs to this set via `_problem_belongs_to_set` — the id must appear in the set's own `result_summary["problems"][*].concept_problem_id` AND the row's `search_space_id` must match the set's — returning 404 on any mismatch (the cross-tenant IDOR fix: a caller who cleared the teacher gate on their own course could otherwise pair a foreign `set_id` with a `problem_id` from a course they don't control). Only once that passes does it read `ConceptProblem.provenance["authored_review"].required`, rebuild a `ReferenceSolutionDraft` from `ocr_draft` or `generated_alt`, then run `build_approved_pair → tag_and_mint → promote` (threading the approved draft's `solution_source` so an approved EXTRACTED OCR reference persists `extracted`); on successful promotion it stamps `approved_reference` and clears the review-required flag. `delete_authored_set` (DELETE) is allowed only in a TERMINAL status (`done`/`failed`); it 409s while the set is `pending`/`indexing`/`provisioning` (`_IN_FLIGHT_STATUSES` in `api.py` is the single source of truth for the non-terminal set) to avoid orphaning Neo4j `:Canon` nodes the in-flight background task writes outside the PG transaction — recovering a dead in-flight run today requires manually marking the set `failed` first (no stuck-run watchdog exists yet). Once past that gate it re-authenticates via `require_course_teacher` on the set's `search_space_id`, deletes the `ConceptProblem`s recorded in `result_summary["problems"]` (removing them from the Tier-2 student selector), deletes the two hidden reference `AITADocument`s (chunks cascade via the `aita_chunks` FK), then the `AuthoredSet` row. FULL KG TEARDOWN for concepts this set ORPHANED (PR4 — the 2026-06-30 audit "delete leaves KG behind" fix): it captures each deleted problem's `concept_id` BEFORE the `ConceptProblem` delete, then a concept is torn down ONLY when it is STRICTLY orphaned — every ambiguous case spares it, because under-tearing-down only leaves KG behind whereas over-tearing-down would 500 or destroy student data. A concept is torn down iff (a) it has ZERO remaining `ConceptProblem`s (checked in-transaction), AND (b) it has NO Postgres student/seed footprint per `_protected_concepts` — no `apollo_sessions.concept_id` (the ONLY `ON DELETE RESTRICT` FK into `apollo_concepts`, so sparing it is what stops `DELETE apollo_concepts` hard-failing the whole delete), no `apollo_learner_state` or `apollo_mastery_events` keyed on the concept's `apollo_kg_entities` (both CASCADE — durable learner beliefs + the append-only grading/refit corpus, written even on the all-`missing`/unresolved path that mints NO `RESOLVES_TO` edge), no `apollo_misconceptions` (a seed-authored bank; CASCADE), and no INBOUND cross-concept prereq from a SURVIVING concept (`from_entity.concept_id NOT IN candidates` — a fellow candidate does NOT spare it, so a whole corrupted set's mutually-linked concepts still clear together), AND (c) its `:Canon` carries NO incoming `RESOLVES_TO` history (`_concepts_with_canon_history` Neo4j read). This union covers EVERY destructive FK the cascade reaches (verified against the migration SQL): the `RESOLVES_TO`-only guard the plan first specified was unsafe — it misses `learner_state`/`mastery_events` and the sessions RESTRICT. For strictly-orphaned concepts ONLY: Postgres deletes `apollo_dedup_decisions` FIRST (its `concept_id` FK is `ON DELETE SET NULL`, so it would otherwise survive) then `apollo_concepts` (cascading `apollo_kg_entities` → `apollo_entity_prereqs`), and Neo4j `_detach_delete_canon` DETACH DELETEs the concept's `:Canon` nodes GUARDED by `WHERE NOT (c)<-[:RESOLVES_TO]-()`. The Neo4j teardown runs AFTER the PG commit (no shared txn — a Neo4j hiccup can't roll back the PG delete) and is idempotent. The response/log gains `removed_concepts`. `get_neo4j_client` is only called when there is at least one unprotected PG candidate, so a spared delete never touches Neo4j. KNOWN LIMITATION (safe direction): a minted-but-rejected problem recorded with `concept_problem_id: None` carries no concept id in `result_summary`, so its concept's KG is not torn down (an under-teardown leak, never data loss).

### Authored problem/solution sets (WU-AAS)

`apollo/provisioning/corpora/` holds assessment corpora for the
reversed-provisioning direction (premade course concept list + question→concept
matching instead of autonomous concept generation); `corpora/calc2/README.md`
documents the 2026-07-07 Calculus 2 assessment (hand-authored 40-concept list,
79 textbook-extracted + 60 original authored problems, blind gpt-5.1 matching
results: ~97% on well-formed text).

**Tier-1 authored-set identity and teardown (2026-07-11).** Structured scraping
stamps every candidate with a content-derived, document-scoped key:
`<document_id>.q<sha256(normalized problem_text)[:32]>`, producing
`problem_code = scrape.<document_id>.q<text_hash32>`. The key is independent of
LLM output order and section/window boundaries, while remaining re-index-safe
because a re-index preserves the document row even when it re-mints chunk rows.
Identical questions emitted by overlapping windows are deduplicated on this key
(first candidate wins). The legacy per-chunk `scrape_questions` path is unchanged.
Old positional rows (`scrape.<64hex>.<ordinal>`) are format-disjoint and inert:
new authored-set runs never look them up or adopt them, so no migration or
read-compatibility shim is required.

Deleting a terminal authored set unions its `result_summary` problem ids with a
set-scoped sweep of every Tier-1 row in the same course whose
`provenance.document_id` equals the set's problem document id. This includes
rejected candidates and dead-run inventory that never received a
`concept_problem_id`; Tier-2 rows and rows owned by other documents are spared.
The existing affected-concept orphan/protection checks apply to the union, and
`removed_problems` counts both referenced rows and swept Tier-1 leftovers.

**Reversed provisioning (2026-07-08, default path).** When a course carries
REGISTERED concepts (a premade list — `scripts/seed_premade_concepts.py`
registers a `concepts.json` into `apollo_subjects`/`apollo_concepts`,
idempotent by hyphen/underscore-normalized slug, backfilling the new
migration-038 `apollo_concepts.description` column and optionally copying
vocab from a subject tree; it NEVER writes problems), the authored-set
orchestrator runs the reversed pipeline instead of the legacy LLM-tag-draft
path (`APOLLO_REVERSED_PROVISIONING=0` is the kill switch; a course with no
registered concepts keeps legacy behavior automatically):

1. **Concept match** — `apollo/provisioning/concept_match.py::match_concept
   (problem_text, concepts, *, chat_fn) -> ConceptMatch` classifies each
   scraped problem against `curriculum_db.list_registered_concepts(db,
   search_space_id=...)` (ALL registered concepts incl. problemless ones,
   provisional-inventory excluded, `description` carried) with one main-tier
   call at `reasoning_effort='low'` (`MeteredChat.cheap/main` now take an
   optional `reasoning_effort`, omitting `temperature` when set), retrying
   ONCE at `'medium'` on an unparseable response, a hallucinated slug, or the
   known self-contradiction slip (primary=NO_MATCH while the rationale names a
   listed concept). NO_MATCH is NEVER force-matched: the candidate is held
   (`reason="no_matching_concept"`, `provenance.authored_review.concept_match`
   records the evidence) and its approve call 409s until the teacher extends
   the course list and re-uploads. Protocol + measured accuracy (95.0% low /
   96.7% with retry): `corpora/calc2/authored/results_authored.md`.
2. **Solution-grounded graph derivation** —
   `apollo/provisioning/authored_sets/graph_derivation.py::
   derive_reference_graph(candidate, spans, *, concept_slug,
   concept_display_name, canonical_symbols, normalization_map, chat_fn) ->
   DerivedGraph{reference_solution, target_unknown, symbolic_mappings,
   bound_variables, retried}` replaces the ungrounded generation (48% S1) with
   the dress-rehearsal procedure that authored `apollo/subjects/calculus_2`:
   one main-tier call over problem text + the paired solution's
   `carries_solution=True` spans ONLY (leak guard) + the matched concept's
   vocabulary, validated by the pure `find_derivation_defects` (Problem
   schema; 5–9 nodes; meaningful snake_case ids — entity keys derive from
   entry_type+id; concrete equations parse under BOTH `sympy.sympify` AND
   `parse_zero_form` with a concept-derived `local_dict` so reserved names
   N/S/E/I don't collide; operator-identity/textbook-trig formulas are
   `content.display=true` pedagogical content, never fake zero-forms; no
   variable/equation fragmentation; Kahn's-algorithm `depends_on` acyclicity
   mirroring the campaign judge's `find_structural_defects` — the mint-time
   cycle guard), with ONE defect-feedback retry at `'high'`, then fail-closed
   `DerivationError` (candidate rejected, `diagnostic="derivation_error:
   ..."`). The validator sweeps 0/60 defects on the committed gold corpus.
   The derived draft promotes as `solution_source='extracted'`; its extras
   (`concept_id`=matched slug, `target_unknown`, `symbolic_mappings`,
   `bound_variables`) ride the problem dict into the promoted payload. When
   label/semantic retrieval finds NO solution span the candidate falls
   through to the legacy `find_or_generate` (generated ⇒ held), unchanged.
3. **Deterministic mint** — `tag_and_mint(db, pair, *, chat_fn, embed_fn,
   resolved_concept: ResolvedConcept | None = None)`: with `resolved_concept`
   (the matcher's `{concept_id, slug}`) there is NO tag-draft LLM call and NO
   concept creation (a missing registered row is a fail-closed
   `TagMintError`), and prereq edges are derived from the reference graph's
   `depends_on` (step X depends_on Y ⇒ `apollo_entity_prereqs` (from=X,
   to=Y) — exactly the DEPENDS_ON edges the S1 driver reads), replacing the
   LLM prereq draft that produced reversed/spurious edges. All downstream
   guards (resolvable-key, concept-scope, acyclicity, writer re-check) run
   unchanged; `resolved_concept=None` is byte-identical to the legacy path.
4. **Transactional mint+promote** — in BOTH the orchestrator and the approve
   path, `tag_and_mint` + gate-8 dup-hash read + `promote` ride ONE
   `begin_nested()` savepoint; a lint rejection raises the internal
   `MintRejected` to unwind it, so the mint's flushed
   concept/KGEntity/prereq/dedup rows never survive as orphans (fixes the
   verified 17→33 entity doubling where mint ran BEFORE the gate-8 check
   with no rollback). `CanonProjectionError` still propagates run-level (PG
   rolls back with the savepoint; the `:Canon` MERGE is idempotent +
   node-only).
5. **Lint gate annotations (additive, anchor-invariant)** — gate 6 skips
   equation steps carrying `content.display=true` (an UNMARKED malformed
   equation still rejects); gate 7 subtracts the graph's top-level
   `bound_variables` (read off the RAW dict — pydantic drops extras) before
   the under-determination check, covering function-valued answers
   (antiderivative argument x, series index n), sampled values f0..fn,
   undetermined coefficients A/B/C, and error-bound symbols. Absent
   annotations ⇒ byte-identical legacy behavior; the fluid+macro anchor suite
   is untouched. `apollo/provisioning/tests/test_lint_calc2_compat.py` pins
   all 60 committed calc-2 gold graphs lint-PASS under the annotations the
   derivation emits (pre-change baseline: 37/60 — 5× gate 6 on display
   identities, 18× gate 7 on function-valued answers).

Eval harness: `campaign/scripts/eval_authored_calc2.py` (bootstrap teacher +
course; upload the 6 corpora HW pairs through the real HTTP path with NO
auto-approve; write `match_report.json` — accuracy vs the corpus's private
`concept_slug` — and `graph_diff_report.json` — per-graph structural diff vs
the committed gold graphs via the pure helpers in
`campaign/scripts/diff_generated_vs_authored.py`; print the `run_s1_s2`
command over the matched concept ids). Acceptance bar: match ≥ 0.95, zero
opaque ids, S1 ≥ 0.95, live teach-back crediting comparably to the authored
counterpart.

WU-AAS is a paired-document provisioning path under
`apollo/provisioning/authored_sets/`. It indexes a teacher's problem PDF and,
when uploaded, a paired solution PDF as hidden `AITADocument` rows, scrapes
candidate problems from the problem doc, and grounds each reference solution
only against the paired solution doc when one exists. A solution PDF is
OPTIONAL (PR B, 2026-07-11): the intended teacher flow is problem-only upload,
with the pipeline auto-generating reference solutions that stay
held-for-review until teacher approval — this policy is unchanged by PR B,
only made reachable without a teacher having to supply a throwaway/duplicate
solution file. The package is split by seam: `indexing.py` reuses the shared
PDF/indexing core, `label_match.py` extracts deterministic printed problem
labels, `paired_retrieval.py` returns doc-scoped `GroundingSpan`s —
`carries_solution=True` only for a label-matched span (a confirmed printed
solution for that problem), `carries_solution=False` for the semantic top-k
fallback (an unconfirmed guess that still rides along as generation context)
— `verification.py` compares low-confidence OCR extractions against an
independently generated draft, `orchestrator.py` runs the per-candidate
promote/hold/reject loop, and `api.py` exposes the teacher HTTP surface.

Pairing state lives in `apollo_authored_sets` via `AuthoredSet`: one
`search_space_id,set_index` row stores the problem document id and the
(nullable) solution document id, set status
(`pending|indexing|provisioning|done|failed`), and bounded `result_summary`
JSON. Candidate results are `promoted`, `rejected`, or `held_for_review`, each
with `outcome`/`diagnostic`/`reason` fields; the per-set `GET
/apollo/authored-sets/{set_id}` returns `result_summary` with the full
`problems` list (not just `promoted` rows), so rejected and
held_for_review candidates are visible to the teacher UI as a review
queue — `test_get_authored_set_surfaces_rejected_and_held_for_review` (PR B4)
pins this. Each `problems` entry whose `ConceptProblem` row still exists is
additionally ENRICHED in the response (review-UI surface, 2026-07-11;
`_enrich_problem_reviews` — the stored row/`result_summary` are never mutated)
with `problem_text` (from the row's payload, capped to `_LIST_OCR_TEXT_CAP`
chars with a `problem_text_truncated` flag — the same size discipline as the
page-evidence surface) and a WHITELISTED `review` projection of
`provenance["authored_review"]`: the CURRENT `required` flag (flips false on
approval, so the UI recomputes displayed counts from live problem state instead
of trusting the frozen `counts`), `reason`, `approved_reference`, and — only
while the hold is active — `ocr_draft`/`generated_alt` each trimmed to
`solution_source` + `reference_solution` (grounding spans, `concept_match`,
`ocr_confidence`, and every other provenance key are deliberately NOT exposed).
Entries with no `concept_problem_id`, a since-deleted row, or malformed shape
pass through unchanged, so pre-enrichment sets keep their old response shape
(`test_get_authored_set_enriches_held_problem` and its sibling tests pin the
whitelist, the cap, the post-approval draft omission, and null-safety). `solution_source='extracted'` means a paired,
label-matched solution span was used; trusted extracted references may
